href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>President Donald Trump said he would support a larger stimulus package beyond the amounts that both parties have put forward so far.</p><p>\"I would like to see a bigger stimulus package, frankly, than either the Democrats or the Republicans are offering,\" he said in an interview on conservative radio host Rush Limbaugh's program. \"I'm going the exact opposite now.\"</p><p>\"I'd like to see a bigger package,\" he said. \"I'd like to see money going to people.\"</p><p>Trump's remarks come as the White House prepares a $1.8 trillion stimulus package to Democrats, <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/us-policy/2020/10/09/trump-economic-stimulus-pelosi/\">The Washington Post reported.</a> It would be the administration's biggest offer yet and an increase from a $1.6 trillion plan they put forward last week in negotiations between Treasury Secretary Steven Mnuchin and House Speaker Nancy Pelosi.</p><p>\"Covid Relief Negotiations are moving along. Go Big!\" Trump wrote in a tweet.</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;Donald J. Trump  (@realDonaldTrump) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1314593632733847552?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">October 9, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>&#160;</p><p>But it's not yet clear what details vary between their newest plan and the last one. Larry Kudlow, a top Trump economic advisor, told reporters on Friday the new plan would contain another round of direct payments, federal unemployment benefits, small business aid, and an airline rescue without elaborating further.</p><p>Trump <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-ends-stimulus-negotiations-until-after-presidential-election-economic-recovery-2020-10\">abruptly ended the talks</a> with a series of tweets on Tuesday, three days after he urged Congress to pass a stimulus bill. It set off several days of headspinning developments with the White House cutting off talks, only to restart them shortly after and aggressively push for a new federal rescue pacakge.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/house-democrats-stimulus-plan-congress-unemployment-economy-pass-vote-bill-2020-9\">The Democratic economic aid bill</a> includes another round of $1,200 stimulus checks to taxpayers and a revival of the $600 in weekly federal unemployment benefits through the end of January. It also provides aid to cash-strapped state and local governments, as well as small businesses.</p><p>But Trump's demands for a larger package collide with the economic inclinations of many Republicans. Many GOP senators opposed a $1 trillion spending plan earlier this summer, citing their concern over the swelling deficit. It's not clear how much support a deal struck between Pelosi and Mnuchin would draw from Republicans on Capitol Hill.</p><p>\"I've got a significant percentage of my members who think we've done enough and who are alarmed by the amount of national debt,\" Senate Majority Leader Mitch McConnell said at a campaign event in Kentucky Thursday. He threw cold water on Friday <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/mitch-mcconnell-stimulus-package-unlikely-three-weeks-trump-economy-odds-2020-10\">regarding the prospect of a stimulus package</a> before the election.</p><p>Many experts are urging lawmakers to approve more federal spending as the economy shows signs of slowing down. The US still hasn't recovered half the jobs it lost in March and April, and permanent layoffs are rising. The unemployment rate stands at 7.9%.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Scott Tipton in the Republican primary to advance to the general election.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Democrat <strong>Diane Mitsch Bush</strong> will face off against Republican <strong>Lauren Boebert</strong> in Colorado's 3rd Congressional District.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Boebert, a staunch conservative, is the owner of Shooters Grill, a Colorado restaurant aptly located in Rifle, Colorado that has its waitstaff open-carry firearms during service.</p><p>In a major upset in June, she defeated 5-term incumbent Rep. Tipton in the Republican primary by about 10 percentage points despite a cash disadvantage. In June 2020, she came under scrutiny for her apparent embrace of the QAnon conspiracy theory which has quickly spread across the United States.</p><p>\"Everything that I've heard of Q, I hope that this is real because it only means that America is getting stronger and better, and people are returning to conservative values,\" she said <a href=\"https://coloradosun.com/2020/07/01/lauren-boebert-qanon-gop-colorado/\">according to the Associated Press</a>.</p><p>While she expressed interest in mid-2020, Boebert is currently attempting to distance herself from the conspiracy theory as her campaign gained interest and came under the spotlight.&#160;</p><p>\"We are attempting to put this stupid [QAnon] thing to bed, but it's all some of [Boebert's opponents] have because they are looking for how are they are going to say that she is so popular out there with ordinary people, how are they going to go against her, and they're choosing stuff like this,\" her spokeswoman Laura Carno said in an interview with the <a href=\"https://coloradotimesrecorder.com/2020/08/boebert-trying-to-back-away-from-qanon/29048/\">Colorado Times Recorder</a>.</p><p>In <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cl0f9uFE5lU&feature=youtu.beu.be\">her campaign ads</a>, Boebert emphasizes wanting to serve in Congress to fight against socialism, protect Americans' 2nd Amendment rights, and create jobs in Colorado.&#160;</p><p>Bush is a former tenured professor and Routt County Commissioner. From 2013 to 2017, Bush served in the Colorado House of Representatives for the state's 26th district.</p><p>She defeated seafood executive James Iacino in the 2020 Democratic primary election for the district to move onto the November ballot. Her <a href=\"https://dianeforcolorado.com/on-the-issues/\">campaign is centered on</a> protecting Colorado's environment and access to clean water, lowering prescription drug costs, passing DACA into federal law with congressional action, and ensure reproductive freedoms.</p><p>Bush previously ran against Rep. Tipton in the general election in 2018 where she lost by a margin of <a href=\"https://results.enr.clarityelections.com/CO/91808/Web02-state.222648/#/\">7.9 percentage points</a>.</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Colorado's <a href=\"https://www.govtrack.us/congress/members/CO/3\">3rd Congressional District</a> is located on the western side of the state, fully covering the western border and parts of the state's borders with Wyoming and New Mexico. It includes the cities of Grand Junction, Steamboat Springs, Pueblo, and Durango, as well as the upscale ski resort towns of Aspen and Telluride.&#160;</p><p>For the 2016 presidential election, the district voted for President Donald Trump over Democratic candidate Hillary Clinton in a 52-40 percentage point split of the vote, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/7/9/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\">according to the Daily Kos</a>.</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=CO03&spec=Np;spec=N\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Bush has raised $1.1 million for her campaign, spent $900,000, and currently has $201,000 in cash on hand remaining. Boebert has raised only $151,000 and has spent about $142,000. She has just over $10,000 to spend on her campaign as the November election approaches.</p><h2>What experts say</h2><p>The race between Bush and Boebert is rated as \"leans Republican\" by <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics and the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report</a> and rated as \"likely Republican\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" data-show-header=\"false\">Expanded Coverage Module: Modern minimalist city apartment? New baby's nursery en suite? Whatever your bathroom's scheme or theme, there's a white curtain to match, and chances are the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B076KLKLWD/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_062717_best-shower-curtains-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B076KLKLWD&#38;linkId=2aa6ec8adea1d03de6f45151c15ff261\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">mDesign Waffle Weave Fabric Shower Curtain</a> will fit right in.</p><p>We have millions of standard-issue white curtains to choose from, but this neutral Stone White color is neither too cold nor too warm, so it should feel right at home in most bathrooms. The soft cotton-poly fabric has a slightly weighted heft that lets the curtain drape and hang naturally. And its classic waffle texture feels comforting, fresh, and clean while adding a subtle element of style.&#160;</p><p>This isn't a water-resistant curtain so you'll need a liner, but it's much lower maintenance than an all-natural cloth option. You'll also be able to throw it in a cold wash cycle and a low-heat tumble dry without worrying too much about shrinkage and wrinkles. It comes in the standard 72 x 72-inch size, plus longer 72 x 84 and 72 x 96 options for taller ceilings.</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5f7def8d1e1b3554e64c467a\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f7def8d1e1b3554e64c467a&type=button&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div>\n\tA hookless shower curtain with detachable liner\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f807f34ea74820019ca6319?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Hookless curtains\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Bed Bath &#38; Beyond</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Flex-on rings make the elegant <a href=\"https://go.skimresources.com?id=35871X943606&#38;xs=1&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bedbathandbeyond.com%2Fstore%2Fproduct%2Fhookless-reg-waffle-fabric-shower-curtain-and-snap-in-liner-set%2F3253374%3FbrandId%3D1656\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Hookless Waffle Fabric Shower Curtain and Snap-in Liner Set</a> extra easy to slip on and off the rod, and its snap-on liner doubles the convenience.&#160;&#160;</h3><p>The cool thing about this <a href=\"https://go.skimresources.com?id=35871X943606&#38;xs=1&#38;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bedbathandbeyond.com%2Fstore%2Fproduct%2Fhookless-reg-waffle-fabric-shower-curtain-and-snap-in-liner-set%2F3253374%3FbrandId%3D1656\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Hookless curtain</a> &#8212; aside from its clean, elegant design and its machine-washable 100% polyester fabrication &#8212; is that hanging your curtain has never been faster or less annoying.&#160;&#160;</p><p>The rings on this curtain are designed to flex open, so you can easily slip your curtain onto the rod (or off again) in a matter of seconds. If that time-saving convenience isn't enough to convert you away from hooks forever, the second best thing is that it comes with a detachable liner that snaps onto the curtain and goes inside the tub, so there's no need to deal with a double rod (unless you want to, of course).&#160;</p><p>The curtain is available in a variety of styles, textures, designs, and fabrics (even satin) to match your aesthetic. Just be sure to check the care instructions if you opt for a different fabric, and keep in mind that certain styles only come in a 71 x 74-inch size.</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5f80800a02495a74af2ed103\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f80800a02495a74af2ed103&type=button&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div>\n\tA unique shower curtain\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f807a83ea74820019ca62f7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"best shower curtain\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Society6</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>With thousands of designs to choose from, <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://society6.com/shower-curtains\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Society6</a> is second to none for unique and one-of-a-kind shower curtains by independent artists.</h3><p>Sometimes you want a shower curtain that just blends into your bathroom. But if you want something that stands out, then you'll want to check out the curtains on <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://society6.com/shower-curtains\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Society6</a>.&#160;</p><p>Society6 is a marketplace for creative artists to sell their work on everyday products like phone cases, office supplies, yoga mats, and &#8212; you guessed it &#8212; <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://society6.com/shower-curtains\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">shower curtains</a>. If you've ever spent any time on the hunt for a cool-looking curtain that doesn't involve printed sea creatures, you've probably found yourself on the site, combing through shower-curtain eye candy in every kind of design from fine line illustrations to geometric shapes and gloriously bold pop art.&#160;&#160;</p><p>You'll get to support independent artists like poet <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/morganharpernichols/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Morgan Harper Nichols</a>, who designed this inspiring print, or illustrator and muralist <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/alexbowman/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Alexandra Bowman</a>, who <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://society6.com/product/blue373068_shower-curtain?sku=s6-6827845p34a35v287\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">creates gorgeous watercolor-style prints</a>. And you'll hang up a beautiful, eye-catching piece of art in what's usually an under-decorated space in dire need of a little pizazz<em>. </em>&#160; &#160;</p><p>The shower curtains themselves are made from machine-washable polyester, though some reviewers say the soft material has a plasticky feel to it. One thing to note is that they're only available in the 71 x 74 size, so you'll want to make sure that the bottom won't drag on your bathroom floor before buying.</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5f7df292e155cf13344485e3\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f7df292e155cf13344485e3&type=button&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div>\n\tA shower curtain that feels custom made\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f7df982282c500018c79243?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Barossa design curtain\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07L3LDMQ3/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_062717_best-shower-curtains-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07L3LDMQ3&#38;linkId=4005f876ab2873b04ac1b86d62b8f0e7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Barossa Design Herringbone &#38; Striped Fabric Shower Curtain</a> has an intricate design that will subtly dress up your bathroom.&#160;</h3><p>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07L3LDMQ3/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_062717_best-shower-curtains-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07L3LDMQ3&#38;linkId=4005f876ab2873b04ac1b86d62b8f0e7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Barossa Design Herringbone &#38; Striped Fabric Shower Curtain</a> is priced like a basic fabric liner, but it looks and feels way more luxurious thanks to its sheen and woven texture.&#160;&#160;</p><p>Made from a machine-washable polyester blend, the curtain is water repellant and won't require an additional liner. And thanks to its textural pattern, silky finish, and a shade of white that's on the cooler side, it's a quick way to elevate any bathroom in need of a crisp and clean pick-me-up.&#160;</p><p>With 11 sizes to choose from &#8212; from shower stall options to extra wide and long options &#8212; this curtain might also be the best looking and most precise fit for your bathtub or shower, especially if you have a history of ending up with shower curtains that hang at awkward lengths.</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5f7df971acfefb0a51600a6a\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f7df971acfefb0a51600a6a&type=button&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div>\n\tAn eco-friendly fabric shower curtain\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f7dfadd282c500018c79249?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Quite Town\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">West Elm</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>If you're on the hunt for a sustainable and responsibly-made curtain with clean designs, you'll fall in love with <a href=\"https://quiettownhome.com/pages/canvas\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Quiet Town's Organic Canvas Shower Curtains</a>.</h3><p>Let's cut to the chase: At $148, this isn't the kind of curtain you buy to replace two or three months down the line, but with <a href=\"https://quiettownhome.com/\">Quiet Town</a> &#8212; a small Brooklyn biz started by artists Lisa and Michael Fine &#8212; that's the whole point.&#160;</p><p>Committed to sustainability, the partners set out to make everyday bathroom essentials in a more eco-conscious way: sourcing materials ethically, partnering with manufacturers who value their workers and the environment, and creating only what's needed.&#160;</p><p>For its machine-washable 100% canvas shower curtains, some of which are also <a href=\"https://westelm.e54b.net/c/196318/267856/4336?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.westelm.com%2Fproducts%2Flcl-quiet-town-home-orient-shower-curtain-desert-b2895%2F%3Fpkey%3Dcquiet-town-home%26isx%3D0.0.1396\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">available through West Elm</a>, the cotton is domestically milled and organically grown in the US. Then the curtains are dyed locally and handmade in Brooklyn &#8212; same deal with its ultra-cool <a href=\"https://quiettownhome.com/collections/orient-sun-shower\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">$62 EVA curtain</a>. Beyond making curtains, Quiet Town is currently focusing a large part of its work on solving the plastic liner waste problem, aka how to keep more of them out of landfills since plastic liners are not recyclable &#8212; yet.&#160;</p><p>There's nothing \"assembly line\" about their offerings &#8212; and that's a welcome departure. Quiet Town has already made a splash in the homewares space for its sensible but striking designs using playful colors and minimalist art.&#160;&#160;</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5f7dfa5f97b2553d971b2c5d\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5f7dfa5f97b2553d971b2c5d&type=button&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div>\n\tHow to choose shower curtains\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f7df2a894fce90018f7bab8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Society 6 shower curtains\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Society6</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>First, choose a material that's durable and easy to care for. According to <a href=\"https://www.keinteriorsolutions.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Donna McMahon</a>, there are three main types:</p><ul><li><strong>Natural fabric:</strong> These are your cotton, linen, canvas, hemp, and bamboo blends. A good quality cotton curtain is a top choice for most people, according to McMahon. Simply toss it in the wash on laundry day to keep it in good shape (other fabrics may have specific care instructions, though). The drawback is that they can be expensive &#8212; up to $60 and sometimes more &#8212; and cannot be used without a liner. All-natural cloth curtains need a protective liner to stay dry and mildew-free.</li><li><strong>Polyester and polyblend:</strong> If you're on a budget, curtains made out of polyester are another long-lasting and low-maintenance choice. They're machine washable, quick-drying, and water-repellant, which means they don't need a liner though they can double as one.</li><li><strong>Plastic:</strong> Plastic curtains shouldn't go in the wash and instead must be regularly wiped and scrubbed clean. They're the cheapest option (most are under $20) and tend to be replaced frequently. They're the most waterproof material of the bunch, so they're usually used as liners but can work as standalone curtains too. Be sure to steer away from PVC (polyvinyl chloride), cautions McMahon, which contains a mix of chlorine, phthalates, and other chemicals that give vinyl plastic curtains that pungent headache-inducing smell. Plastic curtains made with PE (polyethylene), PEVA (polyethylene vinyl acetate), and EVA (ethylene vinyl acetate) are safer alternatives, but when in doubt, \"search for 'PVC free' in product descriptions,\" says McMahon.&#160;</li></ul><p>The rest is a matter of your personal taste. Natural fabric curtains drape beautifully and have a more elevated look, and polyester curtains can have a similar soft, woven-fabric feel.</p><p>In terms of colors, patterns, and prints, go with what makes you happy. If you really don't know where to start, McMahon said, \"Pick a curtain design that has a touch of the prominent color in your bathroom tile or other finishes to tie it all together. And if the tones of your bathroom are soft and subtle, a curtain that's bolder in color can be the perfect contrast too.\"</p><p>Keeping it simple with white though will never go out of style &#8212; just think of every hotel bathroom you've ever seen.&#160;&#160;</p><h2>How to measure shower curtains&#160;</h2><p>The standard size that fits most built-in tubs is 72 x 72 inches, but before you add your brand new curtain to your cart, break out the tape measure to make sure you're getting the proper size.&#160;</p><ul><li><strong>Width:</strong> Measure along the entire length of the curtain rod and add 12 inches so the curtain can drape and extend nicely. For reference, the standard bathtub is about 60-inches long. Shower stalls will be narrower and clawfoot tubs will be longer because the curtain needs to fit around a full circular rod, says McMahon. For this, look for 180 x 70, or you can use two 72 x 72-inch curtains.&#160;</li><li><strong>Height:</strong> The curtain height will also vary depending on what kind of shower you have, but generally the bottom hem should float at least one to two inches above the floor. \"This allows air to circulate and prevent mold and mildew growth,\" says McMahon. Measure from below the rod &#8212; or end of the shower curtain hooks &#8212; to the floor, then subtract at least two inches.&#160;</li></ul>\n\tCheck out other bathroom-related guides\n\t\n\t<ul 50-625_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=2UhgxGBDArw:0R_fwaHDuoc:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn60@2020_4/2020/10/09/19-12-47-135_5e9280e4c1df13eb.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/2UhgxGBDArw":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn67@2020_1/2020/10/09/19-12-47-097_15d3065ca432beb0.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602270691427},{"createdTime":"2020-10-10 \"recovered immediately, almost immediately.\" He added that he \"might not have recovered at all from COVID\" were it not for the antibody cocktail.</p><p>Trump's comment was a departure from the way 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>Trump's coronavirus status remains unclear, with <a interview on Friday, Limbaugh noted that Trump had gone on for an hour and 40 minutes without having to pause or collect his thoughts, arguing that the president had recovered.</p><p>Trump also <a href=\"https://apnews.com/article/virus-outbreak-donald-trump-archive-5b7b10a897559eb678310abbd36577c3\">falsely suggested</a> that the therapeutics he took were a \"cure\" for the coronavirus.</p><p>The interview, touted as a \"virtual rally,\" was the president's third lengthy call-in interview in two days. Trump has not appeared on camera since leaving the hospital on Monday beyond a few videos posted on his Twitter account from the White House.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"First-term Rep. Kim Schrier squares off against Republican Jesse Jensen in Washington's 8th Congressional District","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/washington-8th-district-house-election-kim-schrier-jesse-jensen-2020","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f5a898d7ed0ee001e25ea64?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Kim Schrier midterms\" height=\"1092\" width=\"2186\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Then-congressional candidate Kim Schrier addresses the crowd at an election night party for Democrats on November 6, 2018, in Bellevue, Washington.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Elaine Thompson/AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>First-term Rep. Kim Schrier will face Jesse Jensen in Washington's 8th Congressional District.</li>\n<li>The district is located in western Washington and is home to the communities of Auburn, Issaquah, Sammamish, Wenatchee, Ellensburg, and Leavenworth.</li>\n<li>Schrier, pediatrician, is the first Democrat to ever represent the 8th District.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>First-term <strong>Rep. Kim Schrier</strong> looks to defend her seat against Republican <strong>Jesse Jensen</strong> in Washington's 8th Congressional District.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Schrier, the incumbent, is a pediatrician with her own practice. She was spurred to run after being dissatisfied with the performance of her now-predecessor, Dave Reichert, regarding healthcare and the Affordable Care Act. While she originally planned to challenge Reichert, he announced his intent to retire following the end of his term.&#160;</p><p>\"Frankly, if Congress was doing its job, I would not have to run for office. I would be back holding little babies. But times have changed,\" Schrier said to her staffers according to a <a href=\"https://www.seattletimes.com/seattle-news/politics/kim-schrier-a-doctor-makes-health-care-a-centerpiece-of-her-8th-district-campaign-for-congress/\">Seattle Times report</a>.</p><p>Schrier is currently <a href=\"https://schrier.house.gov/about\">the only female physician</a> serving in Congress and also the first Democrat to ever represent the 8th District. In Congress, she serves on the powerful House Committee on Agriculture and the Committee on Education and Labor.&#160;</p><p>Jensen, Schrier's Republican challenger, is a veteran of the US Army where he was an Army Ranger. Following his military service, he worked as the healthcare director for a kidney dialysis company before changing sectors and becoming a senior program manager for Amazon and Microsoft. His <a href=\"https://www.jessejensen2020.com/issues\">campaign platform is centered around</a> ensuring high quality healthcare for veterans, reforming police departments, and protecting the environment.</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Washington's 8th Congressional District is located in the western region of the state and includes all of Chelan and Kittitas counties as well as parts of Douglas, Pierce, and King counties. The district is home to the communities of Auburn, Issaquah, Sammamish, Wenatchee, Ellensburg, and Leavenworth.</p><p>In the 2016 presidential election, the district voted for Democratic nominee Hillary Clinton over now-President Donald Trump in a 48-45 percentage point split of the vote, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/07/09/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\">according to the Daily Kos</a>.</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=WA08WA08\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Schrier has raised $3.2 million for her campaign, substantially more than Jensen's $192,569. Schrier also holds a massive cash on hand advantage over her challenger. She has $2.4 million left to spend as the November election approaches, or 44 times more than Jensen with only $53,000 remaining.</p><h2>What experts say</h2><p>The race between Schrier and Jensen is rated as \"safe Democratic\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>, \"likely Democratic\" by the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report</a>, and \"leans Democratic\" by <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" data-show-header=\"false\">Expanded Conor Lamb</strong> will square off in November against Republican challenger <strong>Sean Parnell</strong> in Pennsylvania's 17th Congressional District.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Lamb is a veteran in the U.S. Marine Corps Reserve and an attorney. He later became a federal prosecutor in the Department of Justice's Pittsburgh office in Pennsylvania's Western District.</p><p>In 2017, Lamb was chosen as the Democratic nominee for a special election in the state's 18th Congressional District after Republican Rep. Tim Murphy resigned following an alleged extramarital affair. Lamb narrowly defeated Republican Rick Saccone by fewer than 500 votes to represent Pennsylvania's former 18th District.</p><p>In 2018, after the state's congressional map was redrawn pursuant to a court order, Lamb chose to run in the 17th Congressional District, where he defeated Keith Rothfus. <a href=\"https://lamb.house.gov/about/committees-and-caucuses\">In Congress</a>, Lamb serves as the Vice-Chair of the House Committees on Veterans Affairs and is on the House Committee on Science, Space, and Technology and the Committee on Transportation and Infrastructure. He's focused his time in Congress both on veterans' issues and economic issues facing Western Pennsylvania, including bolstering the steel industry.&#160;</p><p>Parnell is a veteran of the U.S. Army where he was an Army Ranger. In 2006, Parnell was wounded in a firefight and was forced to medically retire from the military, and was awarded a Purple Heart and two Bronze Stars.</p><p>He is the cofounder of the American Warrior Initiative, a veterans advocacy organization. Parnell's <a href=\"https://seanforcongress.co/issues/\">campaign platform is centered around</a> strengthening border security and picking pro-life judges for the U.S. court systems. Parnell was endorsed by President Donald Trump and <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jLdXtAL76KI\">recently spoke at the 2020 Republican National Convention.</a></p><h2>The district</h2><p>Pennsylvania's 17th Congressional District is located in western Pennsylvania along a small part of the state's southwestern border outside of the city of Pittsburgh. It is home to all of Beaver County, much of Allegheny County, and a small portion of the southwestern tip of Butler County.</p><p>The state's congressional map was redrawn in 2018 after by the Supreme Court of Pennsylvania ruled that the state's previous congressional <a href=\"https://www.inquirer.com/philly/news/politics/pennsylvania-gerrymandering-supreme-court-map-congressional-districts-2018-elections-20180219.html\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"3cc9d94ac9b36bd3899f5991d0210333\">map was unconstitutionally gerrymandered</a> to favor Republicans.&#160;</p><p>Trump would have carried the district under its current boundaries by two points, 49% to 47%, over Hillary Clinton in 2016, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/07/09/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"5f1d181a742686c409d5b5740785019c\">according to the Daily Kos.</a></p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=PA17PA17\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Lamb has raised $2.2 million for his campaign, just under $1 million more than Parnell with $1.2 million. Lamb also holds a fairly sizable cash on hand advantage of his opponent. He currently has $1.3 million left to spend as the November election approaches, or over $400,000 more than Parnell's remaining $870,000.</p><h2>What experts say</h2><p>The race between Lamb and Parnell is rated as \"leans Democratic\" by <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">the Cook Political Report</a> and \"likely Democratic\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>&#160;and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" data-show-header=\"false\">Expanded Coverage Module: He served as the representative for Pennsylvania's 3rd Congressional District for four terms before being redistricted to the 16th Congressional District.&#160;</p><p>In 2018, he narrowly beat out Ronald DiNicola by <a href=\"https://www.electionreturns.pa.gov/General/OfficeResults?OfficeID=11&ElectionID=63&ElectionType=G&IsActive=0p;IsActive=0\">4.3 points</a> — the closest election of his political career.</p><p>Gnibus is a teacher, cancer survivor, and is currently a PhD student at Gannon University. Her <a href=\"https://www.kristyforcongress.com/priorities\">campaign platform</a> is centered around criminal justice reform, combatting climate change, and bringing affordable healthcare to Pennsylvanians.&#160;</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Pennsylvania's 16th Congressional District is located in northwestern Pennsylvania. The district is home to parts of Butler, Crawford, Erie, Lawrence, and Mercer counties as well as the cities of Erie, Sharon, Hermitage, Butler and Meadville.</p><p>The state's congressional map was redrawn in 2018 after by the Supreme Court of Pennsylvania ruled that the state's previous congressional <a href=\"https://www.inquirer.com/philly/news/politics/pennsylvania-gerrymandering-supreme-court-map-congressional-districts-2018-elections-20180219.html\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"3cc9d94ac9b36bd3899f5991d0210333\">map was unconstitutionally gerrymandered</a> to favor Republicans.&#160;</p><p>Trump would have overwhelmingly carried the district under its current boundaries by 18 points, 58% to 40%, over Hillary Clinton in 2016, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/07/09/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"5f1d181a742686c409d5b5740785019c\">according to the Daily Kos.</a></p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=PA16&spec=Np;spec=N\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Kelly has raised $1.65 million for his campaign, over 8 times more than Gnibus' $195,000. Kelly also currently holds a considerable cash on hand advantage over his opponent. He has $1 million left to spend as the November election nears compare to Gnibus with just $58,000 remaining.</p><h2>What experts say</h2><p>The race between Kelly and Gnibus is rated as \"likely Republican\" by the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report</a> and \"safe Republican\" according to <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a> and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" data-show-header=\"false\">Expanded Coverage Module: 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"Twitter is changing some of its features to crack down on political misinformation leading up to the 2020 presidential election","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/twitter-changes-election-political-misinformation-policy-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f80959e4c3b2e0019bba303?format=jpeg\" alt=\"trump twitter\" height=\"1333\" width=\"1778\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Rafael Henrique/SOPA Images/LightRocket via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Twitter is temporarily changing a number of its features to prevent the spread of political misinformation on the platform as the 2020 presidential election draws near.</li>\n<li>Twitter will prompt users to post a comment on a tweet before retweeting it and will prevent tweets liked by people you don't follow from being recommended to you in your timeline, among other changes.</li>\n<li>The changes are designed to have people to think twice before they amplify a tweet that could contain misleading information ahead of and during the November election.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Twitter will start implementing changes in an effort to limit the spread of political misinformation on the platform leading up to the November 3 presidential election.</p><p>Twitter said in a <a href=\"https://blog.twitter.com/en_us/topics/company/2020/2020-election-changes.html\">blog post</a> it will start encouraging users to post a comment on a tweet before they can retweet it, a move designed to prompt more consideration and thought regarding the tweet's topic and to limit how easily a tweet can reach more people. The company said it will start testing this feature for some Twitter users on Friday.</p><p>Twitter will also start preventing tweets that were liked by people you don't follow from showing up on your timeline on the site. \"This will likely slow down how quickly Tweets from accounts and topics you don't follow can reach you, which we believe is a worthwhile sacrifice to encourage more thoughtful and explicit amplification,\" the company said in the blog post.</p><p><a href=\"https://blog.twitter.com/en_us/topics/product/2020/updating-our-approach-to-misleading-information.html\">In May</a>, Twitter said it would add warning labels to tweets that contain potentially harmful misleading information. Now, the company said when someone tries to retweet a post with such a label, Twitter will point them to credible information regarding the topic before they can share it.</p><p>The company will also add additional warning labels and restrictions to tweets with existing misleading information labels that are posted by US political figures, like candidates and accounts run by their campaigns, as well as US-based Twitter accounts that have more than 100,000 followers.</p><p>\"Twitter has a critical role to play in protecting the integrity of the election conversation, and we encourage candidates, campaigns, news outlets and voters to use Twitter respectfully and to recognize our collective responsibility to the electorate to guarantee a safe, fair and legitimate democratic process this November,\" the company said in the blog post.</p><p>The temporary changes will roll out in the coming weeks, and all will be in effect by October 20, lasting \"through at least the end of election week\" in early November.</p><p>The news comes as Twitter, and other social media sites, gear up to police misinformation ahead of the upcoming election. Twitter has already rolled out a series of moves to crack down on false information on its site. The platform announced it was banning political ads on its site <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/twitter-political-ads-ban-new-details-2019-11\">in late 2019</a>, and has added election labels to the accounts of political candidates, among <a href=\"https://blog.twitter.com/en_us/topics/company/2020/2020-election-changes.html\">other changes.</a></p><p>Other tech companies like Facebook are also making changes to prevent the spread of misleading information. Facebook, for example, said it <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/facebook-says-it-will-ban-all-political-ads-after-election-2020-10\">would stop accepting political ads</a> starting the day after the election. It has also banned accounts, groups, and pages <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/qanon-banned-from-facebook-dealing-massive-blow-to-conspiracy-group-2020-10\">associated with the far-right conspiracy theory QAnon</a>.</p><p>One of Twitter's most active users, President Donald Trump, clashed with Twitter after the company began <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/twitter-public-interest-notice-trump-ballot-boxes-2020-8\">cracking down on his tweets in May</a>, adding \"public interest notices\" and fact-checking labels to his posts. The crackdown prompted the president and other Republicans to claim, without evidence, that Twitter and other tech companies <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/republicans-hijack-antitrust-hearing-facebook-google-amazon-conservative-bias-2020-7\">wield anti-conservative bias</a>.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"Four-term incumbent Rep. Roger Williams squares off against Julie Oliver in Texas' 25th Congressional District","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/texas-25th-district-house-election-roger-williams-julie-oliver-2020","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ee8c305f34d057acc0c6d57?format=jpeg\" alt=\"roger williams\" height=\"933\" width=\"1867\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>In this Sept. 1, 2013 file photo, Rep. Roger Williams, R-Texas walks on Capitol Hill in Washington.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Associated Press/Carolyn Kaster</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Rep. Roger Williams will face Julie Oliver in Texas' 25th Congressional District.</li>\n<li>The 25th District is located in central Texas and is home to the counties of Bosque, Burnet, Coryell, Hamilton, Hill, Johnson, Lampasas, and Somervell.</li>\n<li>The two candidates originally faced each other in 2018, when Williams defeated Oliver by 8.7 percentage points of the vote.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Four-term incumbent <strong>Rep. Roger Williams</strong> looks to defend his House seat from Democratic challenger <strong>Julie Oliver</strong> in Texas' 25th Congressional District.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Williams is a former professional baseball player. Following his career playing and coaching baseball, Williams was a fundraiser for then-Gov. George W. Bush.</p><p>He worked as the North Texas chairman for Bush's presidential campaigns in 2000 and 2004, later becoming the campaign's national grassroots fundraising chairman in 2004. Additionally, Williams was appointed by Gov. Rick Perry in 2004 to become <a href=\"https://www.star-telegram.com/news/politics-government/article244385977.html\">Texas' secretary of state</a>, a position he served in until 2007.&#160;</p><p>Wiliams, elected in 2012, is the first Republican to represent the 25th District since its creation in 1983. In Congress, he serves on the House Committee on Financial Services.&#160;</p><p>Oliver, Williams' challenger, spent much of her career in the healthcare industry working on healthcare finance and taxation, including recently on <a href=\"https://www.julieoliver.org/about\">Austin City Council's board of Central Health</a>. Her <a href=\"https://www.julieoliver.org/issues\">campaign platform</a> is centered around implementing a Medicare for All universal healthcare systen, criminal justice reform, including abolishing for-profit prisons, and expanding voting rights.</p><p>Williams and Oliver originally squared off to represent the 25th District in 2018, where Williams defeated Oliver challenger by <a href=\"https://elections.sos.state.tx.us/elchist331_state.htm\">8.7 percentage points</a>.</p><p><a href=\"https://drive.google.com/file/d/1NsW0PTv_M3_y-7F58NM7povZiq8ilhf9/view\">An internal poll</a> conducted for Oliver's campaign from September 2-5 showed Williams leading her by two points, 43% to 41%. An <a href=\"https://twitter.com/PatrickSvitek/status/1301917394710007812\">internal poll conducted for Williams' campaign</a> by Remington Research Group from Septmber 1-2 showed the congressman leading by a much larger margin of 12 points, 52% to 40%.&#160;</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Texas' 25th Congressional District is located in the center of the state, encompassing a stretch of Texas' Hill Country between Austin and the Dallas-Fort Worth area.&#160;</p><p>The district contains part of the city of Austin itself, including the University of Texas' flagship Austin campus, and the counties of Bosque, Burnet, Coryell, Hamilton, Hill, Johnson, Lampasas, and Somervell as well as portions of Bell, Erath, Hays, Tarrant, and Travis counties.<sup id=\"cite_ref-2\"></sup></p><p>In the 2016 presidential election, the 25th District voted for President Donald Trump over Democratic nominee Hillary Clinton by 15 points in a 55-40 percentage point split of the vote, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/07/09/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\">according to Daily Kos</a>.&#160;</p><p>In <a href=\"https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1W_GTNylAZfboZkDeMsJPGlir3aQB64SzlVHjY9Xdnkk/edit#gid=562073942\">Texas' 2018 US Senate election</a>, the district backed GOP Sen. Ted Cruz by five points, 52% to 47%, over Democratic challenger Beto O'Rourke.&#160;</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=TX25TX25\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Williams has raised $1.5 million for his campaign, or more than twice the amount as Oliver with $676,000. Williams also currently holds a substantial cash on hand advantage over his opponent. He has $1.26 million left to spend as the November election approaches, 14 times more than Oliver's $90,000.</p><h2>What experts say</h2><p>The race between Williams and Oliver is rated as \"likely Republican\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>, the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report</a>, and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" source. Then, select the correct input on your TV so that your Fire Stick appears.</p><p><strong>2. </strong>After your Amazon Fire Stick is connected, scroll up two times using your remote until your cursor highlights the \"Home\" tab.&#160;</p><p><strong>3. </strong>Then, scroll to the right and click \"Settings.\"</p><p><strong>4. </strong>In \"Settings,\" scroll to the right and click on the \"My Fire TV\" tab.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e445c074b661b0b8b6906c3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to update Amazon Fire Stick\" height=\"3024\" width=\"3024\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click on &#34;My Fire TV&#34; to look at more information and details about your device.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Taylor Lyles/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>5. </strong>In \"My Fire TV\" click on \"About.\" In \"About\" scroll down and select \"Check for Updates\" to see if your device is up to date. If you see \"Install Update\" that means that there is an update available for your device and you should click it.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e445c213b62b707781420d6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to update Amazon Fire Stick\" height=\"3024\" width=\"3024\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Click on &#34;About&#34; then click &#34;Check for Updates.&#34;\n<p class=\"copyright\">Taylor Lyles/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>6. </strong>Select \"Install Update\" on your remote and your TV should power off. for \"The Boys\" season two finale.</strong></em></p><p>Amazon Prime Video's \"The Boys\" is a massive hit.</p><p>With its second season, which concluded on Friday, the mature superhero series became Amazon's biggest launch for an original series yet and has <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/nielsen-viewership-data-amazons-the-boys-a-major-hit-2020-10\">cracked Nielsen's weekly lists of most-watched streaming titles</a>, the only non-Netflix series to do so.</p><p>This season, episodes were released on a weekly basis, as opposed to the first season when they dropped all at once like Netflix's binge model. Did the new release schedule help spread the word?</p><p>\"Five weeks later, we're still at the forefront of pop culture, which was always the goal,\" showrunner Eric Kripke told Business Insider during a recent interview. \"I do think it turned out to be a good thing in terms of how much longer people are talking about the show.\"</p><p>But Kripke said that the format isn't set in stone for season three, which was greenlit in July, two months before the second season's debut on September 4. A spinoff series about a college for superheroes is also in the works.&#160;</p><p>Kripke also talked to Business Insider about how working on a streaming series differs from a network series like The CW's \"Supernatural,\" which he created; the fate of the Nazi \"superhero\" Stormfront, played by Aya Cash; and why Fresca became a running joke in season two.</p><p><strong><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f5a50f27ed0ee001e25e88c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"the boys 201 homelander\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Antony Starr as Homelander.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Jasper Savage/Amazon Studios</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></strong></p><p><strong>The show seems to be a massive hit, even moreso than last year. Why do you think the show has gained such a larger audience with season two?</strong></p><p>What we've noticed is that a lot of people have been finding season one as so many other people talk about season two. They see so many comments on social media about how crazy the show is which makes others want to catch up. We see a lot of people say they slept on the show for so long but they're watching it now and loving it.</p><p>I'm really grateful. This is the project I've worked on that I'm having the most fun on and think I might love the most. It's the one that most closely represents my sensibilities, so to see it get the reaction that it's getting is really gratifying.&#160;</p><p><strong>What about it makes you love it more than even \"Supernatural\"? I'm sure \"Supernatural\" fans will be upset about that.</strong></p><p><em>[laughs]</em> I love all my children, but I don't have the network restrictions on this that I have on \"Supernatural.\" Anyone who has spent time in the writers room with me can tell you I have a pretty filthy sense of humor and I really enjoy dark comedy and satire. I think it's important to also have a lot of emotion and heart, which \"Supernatural\" does have.</p><p>But those three things really represent what I love: real heart and emotion, satire and dark comedy, and filthiness. I'm allowed to put all of those things in \"The Boys\" in a way I wasn't allowed to with \"Supernatural.\"</p><p><strong>With \"Supernatural,\" you're working in this network framework of 20 episodes. With \"The Boys,\" do you ever find that you're too confined with fewer episodes?</strong></p><p>Dude, it's so much better. When you have eight episodes, you can tell a tighter story. \"Supernatural\" works as a network show because it's ultimately a procedural. In it's own weird way it's a cop show. On \"The Boys,\" you can have every episode move the football forward. It's harder to wrap your head around a 20-episode story.&#160;</p><p>I actually don't work any less on \"The Boys\" than I did on \"Supernatural.\" It's not like it's a vacation. I spend all that extra time on the scripts and making sure the emotions are right versus \"Supernatural,\" which was, lovingly, endless triage. Always racing to write things and throwing it out the door to shoot it. If people knew how chaotic it was to make that show they would be horrified. <em>[laughs]</em></p><p><em><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f68e8bb323fc4001e0d786b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"the boys 204 hq stormfront\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Aya Cash as Stormfront.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Jasper Savage/Amazon Studios</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></em></p><p><strong>When season two first premiered, some fans were upset they couldn't binge the whole series all at once. Now that the whole season is out, are you still glad the episodes were released on a weekly basis? Do you think that helped in driving word of mouth?</strong></p><p>I am glad, but I get why people would be disappointed. We're going to look at the [viewership] data and we'll look at whether it was a good idea or not. That will determine what we do next season.</p><p>Five weeks later, we're still at the forefront of pop culture, which was always the goal. I do think it turned out to be a good thing in terms of how much longer people are talking about the show. I know this may sound selfish, but I spent two years of my life creating this thing and the thought that it would premiere on a weekend and get watched in a week makes me sad. This was a much more gratifying experience for me that people would be able to obsess over all the details we worked so hard on.</p><p><strong>But that format isn't locked in yet for next season?</strong></p><p>No, not yet.&#160;</p><p><strong>How would you define The Church of the Collective and how will it play a factor in season three? And can you describe the obsession with Fresca?</strong></p><p><em>[laughs]&nbsp;</em>I don't want to give too much away but Deep will have a very different relationship with the Church but it will still be a part of the story.</p><p>As far as Fresca, the thing with the show is that it's sometimes really random. We enjoy that. At the beginning of the season, we were talking about what drink the Church would be into. It wouldn't be beer. Then someone said Fresca and we just started laughing. It seems like the proper drink for cult members for no good reason and then we just kept running and running and running with that joke. That will be Fresca's new marketing slogan, they're really excited about that. [<em>laughs]</em></p><p><strong>In the finale, Homelander says that Stormfront is being held in some facility. Is that a lie to cover up that she's dead? Is there a chance we could see more Stormfront?</strong></p><p>She is not dead but no comment about whether we see her again or not. But she's not dead and she's now Stumpfront. It felt like the best punishment for our stumpy little Nazi was not death but for her to end up mutilated for potentially centuries since she ages so slowly. That felt like the best punishment for that character. Hashtag \"Stumpfront Lives.\"</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/5f8065334c3b2e0019bba170?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"553b8c4778bcd6b8827a9bdf747b3eef","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn47@2020_6/2020/10/09/19-12-45-862_c9e34811b79ab433.webp","destWidth":1839,"destHeight":1379,"sourceBytes":50598,"destBytes":50598,"author":"tclark@businessinsider.com (Travis Clark)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/5f5a50f37ed0ee001e25e88d?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn16@2020_6/2020/10/09/19-12-49-051_0390e7c3b917c793.webp","https://i.insider.com/5f5a50f27ed0ee001e25e88c?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn52@2020_6/2020/10/09/19-12-54-262_523c2d4b2122ef37.webp","https://i.insider.com/5f68e8bb323fc4001e0d786b?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn31@2020_1/2020/10/09/19-12-50-515_9834a95b00a65282.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn91@2020_3/2020/10/09/19-12-53-792_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=1JZ9ROcETms:PFC-N2sOVNA:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn76@2020_4/2020/10/09/19-12-49-416_64710140c49718af.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=1JZ9ROcETms:PFC-N2sOVNA:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn55@2020_6/2020/10/09/19-12-55-715_b340756c0b7a71b2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn40@2020_6/2020/10/09/19-12-50-625_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=1JZ9ROcETms:PFC-N2sOVNA:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn70@2020_5/2020/10/09/19-12-50-964_51524b496ef52f4c.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/1JZ9ROcETms":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn52@2020_5/2020/10/09/19-12-46-996_13f91d4d7b97d272.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602270691386},{"createdTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"What are blue-chip stocks? Highly reliable stocks from well-established companies that can add strength and safety to any portfolio","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-are-blue-chip-stocks","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f80abffea74820019ca64a9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"blue chip\" height=\"1499\" width=\"3000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Taking their name from the most valuable poker chips, blue-chip stocks represent the highest-quality companies trading on the market.\n<p class=\"copyright\">zimmytws/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A blue-chip stock is a stock from the market's highest-quality companies, known for their low risk and reliable performance.</li>\n<li>Blue-chip stocks are stable and pay high dividends, but they are typically expensive and don't grow much.</li>\n<li>Blue-chip stocks belong in any well-diversified portfolio, though they tend to be favored by older or more conservative investors.</li>\n</ul>\n<ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/investing-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\"><strong>Visit Insider's Investing Reference library for more stories</strong></a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\"><strong>.</strong></a></li>\n</ul><p>Investing sometimes gets compared to gambling — something prudent investors and financial pros deny, naturally. But the stock market <em>has</em> borrowed one bit of lingo from casinos and card games: blue-chip stocks.</p><p>Just as blue chips in poker hold the highest value, so do blue-chip stocks in the stock market. They represent the crème de la crème of equities — the biggest, richest companies. Many of them are household names.&#160;</p><p>Blue-chip stocks provide a way to invest in stable, good-performing corporations with minimal risk. Plus, they usually pay good dividends.</p><h2>What are blue-chip stocks?&#160;</h2><p>Blue-chip stocks occupy the most venerated strata of the stock market. As leaders in their industries, these companies have strong histories — some are over 100 years old — and deliver consistently strong performance. Whether the market overall is up or down, blue chips prove themselves as steady and reliable investments. As a result, their share prices tend to be high.</p><p>The blue-chip term came into financial parlance in the early 1920s. According to Wall Street lore, it was coined by a journalist for Dow Jones, Oliver Gingold, as he watched a stock tape ticker reporting trades of shares valued at $200 or more. He promptly dubbed these companies \"blue-chip stocks.\"</p><h2>What makes a stock a blue chip?&#160;</h2><p>No official guidelines exist around the size and value of blue-chip companies. But they do share some characteristics:</p><ul><li><strong>Large market capitalization</strong>: Blue chips tend to be huge, well-financed corporations. Their market capitalization — that is, the total market value of all their outstanding shares — is in the high billions, putting them in the category of large-capitalization (or large-cap) stocks. The cheapest of these large caps enjoy a value of at least $5 billion; most are north of $10 billion.</li><li><strong>Growth history</strong>: Blue-chip companies display years, sometimes decades, of sustained growth and ongoing prospects. Their share prices rarely jump dramatically, but they can show steady appreciation over time.&#160;</li><li><strong>Stock index</strong>: Blue chips occupy positions in the major market indexes: the Dow Jones Industrial Average (DJIA), the S&#38;P 500, the Nasdaq 100. A company is often seen to have \"made it,\" blue-chip status-wise, if on one of these lists, which act as bellwethers for the stock market itself.</li><li><strong>Dividends</strong>: While not always a feature, many blue chips pay shareholders a good, steady dividend. As mature companies, blue chips focus less on growth than start-ups and other businesses that need to continually seed development. For blue-chips, the freed up cash flow allows companies to share profits with stock owners through dividend payments. As profit margins grow, the dividends often increase as well.&#160;</li></ul><h2>Blue-chip stock list&#160;</h2><p>Blue-chip stocks include notable names familiar to almost everyone, a trait attributable either to their long histories or to their positions as industry leaders (or both). Some of them include:&#160;</p><ul><li>Alphabet (GOOGL)</li><li>Amazon (AMZN)</li><li>American Express (AXP)</li><li>Apple (AAPL)</li><li>Bank of America (BAC)</li><li>Coca-Cola (KO)</li><li>Costco (COST)</li><li>Home Depot (HD)</li><li>IBM (IBM)</li><li>Johnson &#38; Johnson (JNJ)</li><li>McDonald's (MCD)</li><li>Microsoft (MSFT)</li><li>Starbucks (SBUX)</li><li>Visa (V)</li><li>Walmart (WMT)</li></ul><h2>Benefits of blue-chip stocks&#160;</h2><p>Investors find a number of benefits in buying shares of blue-chip companies. These include:</p><ul><li><strong>Low volatility</strong>: As big corporations, blue-chip companies benefit from economies of scale and also enjoy revenue streams from multiple products and services. While not immune from <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-a-recession\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">economic downturns</a>, well-established blue chips are not easily shaken, even in times of market volatility.</li><li><strong>Dependability and transparency</strong>: With their long histories and status as industry leaders, blue chips operate with seasoned management teams. The companies' fame and high profiles tend to keep their operations transparent.</li><li><strong>Rich income</strong>: Steady earnings without a need to invest heavily in growth means blue chips can provide steady, strong dividend payments. Next to US Treasuries, blue-chip dividends are the most reliable go-to for income-oriented investors.</li></ul><h2>Drawbacks of blue-chip stocks</h2><p>On the flip side, the blue-chip features that work as benefits for some investors act as deterrents for others.</p><ul><li><strong>Low growth</strong>: Unless you invested in one decades ago, you won't make a killing in blue-chip stocks. These are mature companies, for the most part — their big-growth days are behind them. They appreciate steadily, but not dramatically. That's the trade-off for their low risk.&#160;</li><li><strong>Expensive: </strong>No bargains here — blue-chip stocks have been discovered. Because blue chips play in the large-market cap sandbox, the price to buy in on a single share often runs a couple hundred dollars or more. For many younger investors, the share cost far exceeds the level needed to acquire a stock position of any significant size.&#160;</li><li><strong>Strong but not invulnerable: </strong>Sometimes a sterling reputation can hide the fact that a blue chip is resting on its laurels and failing to innovate. Monolithic corporations can be slow to respond to changing times, consumer demands, and industry trends. Though it happens rarely, blue chips can and do go bankrupt: General Motors and Lehman Brothers are two recent examples.&#160;&#160;</li></ul><h2>What is the blue-chip index?</h2><p>Investors seeking exposure to those companies considered most valuable often turn to indexes as a way to slice a piece of the blue-chip pie. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/etf-vs-mutual-fund\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Exchange-traded funds</a> and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/personal-finance/how-to-invest-in-index-funds-explained\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">index (mutual) funds</a> focus provide an entry point into blue-chip investing without the cost-prohibitive price.</p><p>These funds basically track \"blue-chip indexes\" — that is, the major stock exchange indexes that include individual blue-chip stocks: the Dow Jones Industrial Average, the S&#38;P 500, and the Nasdaq-100. The funds cherry-pick from the exchanges to populate their portfolios with industry blue chips.&#160;</p><p>Across the pond, the New Europe Blue Chip Index tracks 30 of the top stocks traded on the Continent. The DAX Index tracks the top 30 companies on the Frankfurt Stock Exchange.</p><h2>The financial takeaway</h2><p>The security of blue chips ranks at the top of their appeal to investors. Blue chips' history of weathering even the stormiest of times puts them in a kind of safe-haven category. This gives investors comfort in knowing these stocks emerge less scathed than their counterparts in <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-a-bear-market\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">rocky times</a>.&#160;</p><p>These stock-market stalwarts look especially attractive to older investors, who are often risk-averse, dislike volatility, and seek income from their investments. More often than not, younger investors, who want bigger growth and can take chances, avoid blue chips for these very reasons: the lack of flash and hype, and the high price of their shares.&#160;</p><p>Still, while the weighting varies based on their goals and risk tolerance, all investors can rely on blue-chip stocks as a means to add strength and stability to their portfolios.&#160;</p><h2>Related Coverage in&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/investing-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\">Investing</a>:</h2><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/personal-finance/why-invest-stock-market\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Why invest in the stock market? Because it can be more dangerous not to</a></h3><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/personal-finance/how-to-invest-in-stocks-beginners-guide\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">How to invest in stocks, even if you're starting from scratch</a></h3><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/personal-finance/how-to-start-investing\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">How to start investing at any age, according to financial planners who know</a></h3><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/personal-finance/warren-buffett-recommends-index-funds-for-most-investors\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Warren Buffett thinks index funds are the best way for everyday investors to grow their money — here's how you can start</a></h3><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-are-penny-stocks\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-position=\"1\" data-analytics-module=\"featured_post\">Penny stocks are cheap and often see massive gains, but they're also very risky. with a code first.</p><p>This can easily be done from your <a rel=\"nofollow\">PlayStation 4 (From $299.99 at Best Buy)</a></h4><h2><strong>How to redeem a gift card code on your <a href=\"http://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?subId1=bi_102519_redeem-code-on-ps4&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fsony-playstation-4-1tb-fortnite-neo-versa-console-bundle-jet-black%2F6360910.p%3FskuId%3D63609100910\" This should be a registered account with internet access.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5db31720dee019310e189903?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to redeem code on PS4\" height=\"1080\" width=\"1920\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The PlayStation store is accessible from the main menu.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ross James/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>2.</strong> From the PlayStation 4's Store menu, scroll down to the second-to-last option, \"Redeem Codes,\" and select it.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5db3174cdee019319e39d45a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to redeem code on PS4\" height=\"1080\" width=\"1920\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>It takes a bit of scrolling, so you might not see the &#34;Redeem Codes&#34; option at first.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ross James/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.</strong> Your voucher should have come with a 12-digit code that you can now enter into this box. If the code was bought as a digital purchase, like through Amazon, you might only have the code in an email. An example code will look something like: \"94GP-QTNL-KKNN.\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5db31776dee01939e57be6e7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to redeem code on PS4\" height=\"1080\" John Carter squares off against Democrat Donna Imam in Texas' 31st Congressional District","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/texas-31st-district-house-election-john-carter-donna-imam-2020","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f5a756c7ed0ee001e25e9bf?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Rep. John Carter\" height=\"1827\" width=\"3653\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Rep. John Carter, R-TX., leaves the House Republican Conference meeting, beginning at the Capitol Hill Club on Wednesday, August 1, 2012.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Bill Clark/CQ Roll Call/</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Rep. John Carter will face Democratic challenger Donna Imam in Texas' 31st Congressional District.</li>\n<li>The district is located in central Texas and is home to Austin's northern suburbs and Fort Hood.</li>\n<li>Carter is the first and only person to represent the 31st District, which was established in 2003.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Nine-term incumbent <strong>Rep. John Carter</strong> looks to defend his House seat against Democratic challenger <strong>Donna Imam&#160;</strong>in Texas' 31st Congressional District.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Carter is an attorney and formerly an elected judge for the state's 277th District Court, a position he held for five terms. He retired from his position in 2001 after the 31st Congressional District was created.</p><p>He currently sits in the House Committee on Appropriations where he is a ranking member of the Subcommittee on Military Construction, Veterans Affairs, and Related Agencies. He is also the co-chairman of the House Army Caucus.</p><p>The nine-term incumbent, Carter, is the only person to ever represent the 31st District since its creation after the 2000 US Census.</p><p>Imam, Carter's Democratic challenger, is an entrepreneur and engineer. She currently works for ProductCamp Austin, an education nonprofit. Her campaign <a href=\"https://votefordonna.com/#solutions\">platform is centered around</a> expanding healthcare access for all, education access for all, and a path to citizenship for DACA recipients.</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Texas' 31st Congressional District is located in central Texas. The district is home to Williamson County and a part of Bell county. It includes the northern Austin suburbs as well as the Fort Hood United States Army post.&#160;</p><p>The 31st District was formed in 2003 and is one of two districts in the state of Texas which has never been represented by a Democrat.</p><p>In the 2016 presidential election, the district voted for President Donald Trump over Democratic nominee Hillary Clinton in a 54-41 percent split of the vote, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/07/09/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\">according to Daily Kos Elections</a>.</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=TX31TX31\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Carter has raised about $1.6 million for his campaign so far, or over six times more than Imam's $249,000. Carter also holds a substantial cash on hand advantage over his opponent. He has $922,000 left to spend on his campaign as the November election approaches, or close to $880,000 more than Imam with just $42,099 remaining.</p><h2>What experts say</h2><p>The race between Carter and Imam is rated as \"safe Republican\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a> and \"likely Republican\" by <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">the Cook Political Report</a> and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" data-show-header=\"false\">Expanded Coverage Module:
