style=\"color: #222222;\">.</strong></li></ul><hr><p><br>JPMorgan Private Bank's head of US equity strategy told Bloomberg on Friday that the stock market won't see the bullish outcome it's expecting from a Joe Biden victory unless there's a full blue wave outcome.</p><p>\"It does appear increasingly likely that we see a blue wave and I think that is what the market is pricing in right now when you see equities continue to move,\" Monica DiCenso said.</p><p>The strategist explained that it will be much harder for Biden to pass a large stimulus bill without Democratic control of the Senate, and said: \"I really do think you probably need the blue wave for the real bullish outcome that many people are talking about to come to fruition.\"&#160;</p><p>DiCenso added that the stimulus, combined with continued low interest rates, will be the \"perfect backdrop for equities over the near to intermediate term.\"</p><p>While some investors are nervous that a blue wave will be negative for stocks because Biden's corporate tax hikes will crush company earnings, DiCenso said the stimulus spending will offset higher taxes.</p><p><strong><em>Read more:</em></strong><em> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/investing-strategy-and-stock-picks-from-fund-manager-brandon-nelson-2020-10\" data-analytics-position=\"2\" data-analytics-module=\"\">Fund manager Brandon Nelson is tripling his benchmark in 2020 with 'less-discovered' companies that become big winners. Here are 3 themes and 9 stocks he's betting on.</a></em></p><p>The strategist suggested investors seek out cyclical stocks like industrials and healthcare to prepare for this outcome.&#160;</p><p>\"Focus on sectors that would benefit from the stimulus spending and just stimulating the economy in general that might offset some of the impact of the rollback of tax cuts,\" she said.&#160;</p><p>Industrial stocks have outperformed in the last few months and will probably continue to outperform, she said. The health care sector tends to be defensive and is also innovating on the vaccine front right now. \"It's a great place to hide if you're a little worried but want some leverage to the innovation story,\" DiCenso added.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"Suspects accused of targeting Michigan Gov. Gretchen Whitmer have a history of ties to self-styled militias. Here's what you need to know about these extremist groups.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-you-need-know-extremist-groups-tied-to-whitmer-conspiracy-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f808b9cea74820019ca63cf?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Coronavirus lockdown protest Michigan\" height=\"2666\" width=\"3555\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>People take part in a protest for &#34;Michiganders Against Excessive Quarantine&#34; at the Michigan State Capitol in Lansing, Michigan on April 15, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.gettyimages.com/detail/news-photo/people-take-part-in-a-protest-for-michiganders-against-news-photo/1210050142?adppopup=true\" target=\"_blank\">Jeff Kowalsky/AFP via Getty Images</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Federal prosecutors on Thursday <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/fbi-foiled-right-wing-militia-plot-kidnap-michigan-gretchen-whitmer-2020-10\">charged six men on suspicion of conspiring</a> to kidnap the Michigan Gov. Gretchen Whitmer and incite violence against the government.&#160;</li>\n<li>Many of these members have a history of ties to anti-government, extremist movements.&#160;&#160;</li>\n<li>Here's what you need to know about the so-called militias that are associated with the men charged in the Whitmer case.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Federal prosecutors on Thursday <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/fbi-foiled-right-wing-militia-plot-kidnap-michigan-gretchen-whitmer-2020-10\">charged six men on suspicion of conspiring</a> to kidnap the Michigan Gov. Gretchen Whitmer. According to an FBI affidavit, the suspects \"agreed to unite others in their cause and take violent action against multiple state governments that they believe are violating the U.S. Constitution,\" and in the process as part of their \"recruitment effort\" reached out to \"a Michigan based militia group.\"&#160;</p><p>Far-right agitators have expressed anger after Whitmer carried out a statewide lockdown in wake of the COVID-19 pandemic. Hundreds of people, many of them armed, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/michigan-lockdown-protesters-brought-rifles-into-the-state-capitol-2020-4\">descended on the state capitol</a> last spring.</p><p>Emboldened by President Donald Trump who publicly embraced the groups, calling them <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-protestors-with-guns-in-michigan-capitol-are-very-good-people-2020-5\">\"very good people,\"</a> they occupied government property while carrying signs denouncing Whitmer and the measures meant to slow the spread of COVID-19 .</p><p>Trump also posted a series of tweets to \"Liberate\" several US states in lockdown, which was <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-liberate-tweets-are-hailed-by-far-right-extremists-nbc-2020-4\">hailed by far-right social media users</a> as support for the anti-government movement.&#160;</p><p>Many of these members have been tracked to a history of ties to anti-government, extremist factions.&#160;&#160;Here's what you need to know about the extremist anti-government groups linked to the men charged in the Whitmer case:</p>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\tThe Michigan Attorney General and authorities have accused the men of being part of a so-called militia group called the 'Wolverine Watchmen'\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f808b0aea74820019ca63c4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"AP20275779242360\" height=\"1665\" width=\"2221\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Michigan Attorney General Dana Nessel in March\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP Photo/David Eggert</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Michigan Attorney General Dana Nessel <a href=\"https://www.michigan.gov/ag/0,4534,7-359-92297_99936-541891--,00.html\">announced anti-terrorism charges against the men,</a> who are accused of being members or associates of the self-styled \"Wolverine Watchmen\" militia.</p><p>In an affidavit supporting the state's complaint, Brian Russell, a Michigan Department of State Police Detective Sergeant <a href=\"https://www.michigan.gov/documents/ag/Affidavit_paul_bellar_704642_7.pdf\">described the suspects</a> \"an anti-government, anti-law enforcement, militia group who have performed tactical training\" and \"made terroristic threats towards government officials and organizations and provided material support for planned acts of terrorism.\"</p><p>The suspects are accused of having recruited members for the Wolverine Watchment via Facebook since last November.</p>\n\tThe 'boogaloo' movement is a far-right, anti-government movement that has been charged with domestic terrorism\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f808b36ea74820019ca63c8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"boogaloo boys\" height=\"683\" width=\"910\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A member of the far-right militia, Boogaloo Bois, walks next to protesters demonstrating outside Charlotte Mecklenburg Police Department Metro Division 2 just outside of downtown Charlotte, North Carolina, on May 29, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">LOGAN CYRUS/AFP via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>The \"boogaloo\" movement <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/boogaloo-bois-protest-far-right-minneapolis-extremist-guns-hawaiian-shirts-2020-5\">comprises a far-right group</a> that researchers from the Middlebury College's Center on Terrorism, Extremism, and Counterterrorism has <a href=\"https://www.middlebury.edu/institute/academics/centers-initiatives/ctec/ctec-publications-0/boogaloo-movement-wants-be-seen-anti-racist\">described as</a> \"the breaking point where government oppression is finally met with revolutionary violence from armed citizens.\"</p><p><a href=\"https://www.insider.com/boogaloo-bois-protest-far-right-minneapolis-extremist-guns-hawaiian-shirts-2020-5\">Business Insider previously reported</a> that \"some members use Neo-Nazi symbols at protests, including the skull balaclava, suggesting that white nationalists have identified with aspects of the loose movement.\"</p><p>The group, which organizes its activities online, began <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/boogaloo-bois-protest-far-right-minneapolis-extremist-guns-hawaiian-shirts-2020-5\">on 4chan's white supremacist and libertarian message boards.</a> In June, Facebook called the group a \"dangerous organization\" and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/facebook-bans-hundreds-of-groups-users-linked-to-boogaloo-movement-2020-7\">banned the movement from its platform</a>, removing hundreds of accounts and over 100 linked groups.&#160;</p><p>In June, three self-proclaimed members of the \"boogaloo\" movement <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/3-boogaloo-men-terror-charges-george-floyd-protest-riot-conspiracy-2020-6\">were arrested on domestic terrorism charges</a> on suspicion of planning to spark violence during anti-racism protests. That same month, the Department of Homeland Security said \"domestic terrorists advocating for the boogaloo very likely will take advantage of any regional or national situation involving heightened fear and tensions to promote their violent extremist ideology and call supporters to action.\"</p><p>That came after an intelligence assessment from the National Capital Region Threat Intelligence Consortium, which <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/far-right-boogaloo-extremists-may-attack-washington-dc-intelligence-assessment-2020-6\">warned that the boogaloo may target Washington, DC.</a></p>\n\tOne of the men was wearing a hat and a sweatshirt bearing an emblem of the 'Three Percenters,' a self-styled anti-government militia.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f808b634c3b2e0019bba2c4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Screenshot_2020 06 03 r orangecounty   OC Sheriff deputy forgoing his name badge to wear a patch promoting the far right, r[...]\" height=\"862\" width=\"1150\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A sheriff&#39;s deputy in Costa Mesa, California, donning patches for the Oath Keepers and Three Percenters movement.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Screen capture/Reddit</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>The Three Percenters are an <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/the-three-percenters-militia-group-protecting-gop-lawmakers-in-oregon-2019-6\">anti-government, anti-gun regulation group</a> that formed in 2008. The group was photographed guarding the <a href=\"https://qz.com/1053604/who-were-the-armed-camouflaged-men-in-charlottesville-who-have-nothing-to-do-with-the-military/\">2017 white-supremacist \"Unite the Right\" rally in Charlottesville</a>.&#160;</p><p>\"The reference to 3 percent stems from the dubious historical claim that only 3 percent of American colonists fought against the British during the War of Independence,\" <a href=\"https://www.splcenter.org/fighting-hate/extremist-files/ideology/antigovernment\">according to the Southern Poverty Law Center, </a>which identifies the group as an anti-government militia movement.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.nbcnews.com/tech/tech-news/whitmer-conspiracy-allegations-tied-boogaloo-movement-n1242670\">NBC News</a> reported Barry Croft, one of the men charged in the Whitmer case, wore a \"tricorn hat and a sweatshirt with the insignia of the Three Percenters,\" had a history of involvement in self-styled militias, and \"pushed pro-Trump conspiracy theories that absolved Russia of meddling in the 2016 election.\" Adam Fox, who was also charged, had a Facebook profile picture with a Three Percenter label, according to NBC News.</p>\n\tOne of the men charged in the alleged plot against Gov. Whitmer was part of an anti-lockdown Facebook group.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f808b804c3b2e0019bba2c5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"michigan lockdown protests\" height=\"1500\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A militia group with no political affiliation from Michigan stands in front of the Governors office after protesters occupied the state capitol building during a vote to approve the extension of Governor Gretchen Whitmer&#39;s emergency declaration/stay-at-home order due to the coronavirus disease (COVID-19) outbreak, at the state capitol in Lansing, Michigan, U.S. April 30, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters/Seth Herald</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Adam Fox was a member of a public Facebook group called \"Open Michigan,\" according to NBC News. Early in the pandemic, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-life-is-like-michigan-home-viral-anti-lockdown-protests-2020-5\">anti-lockdown protests, many of them armed</a>, flooded states including Michigan. Many of these protests were organized in Facebook groups, which <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/facebook-groups-anti-quarantine-protests-states-violations-remain-despite-removals-2020-4\">prompted the social media platform to remove posts</a> that defied state government orders.&#160;<br /><br />Michigan Attorney General Dana Nessel told Business Insider that these men who were charged with conspiring against Whitmer <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/michigan-attorney-general-dana-nessel-discusses-trump-far-right-violence-2020-10\">may have been emboldened by President Donald Trump's rhetoric.&#160;</a></p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;Donald J. Trump  (@realDonaldTrump) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1251169217531056130?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">April 17, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>&#160;</p><p>\"And so their gripes, their complaints with the government seemed to be further legitimized by the fact that you have elected leaders [supporting them] &#8212; and in one case, of course, the commander-in-chief of our nation, putting things on his social media feed saying 'liberate Michigan,'\" Nessel said.&#160;<br /><br />\"These guys think that he's talking to them. He actually said, you recall, that the governor ought to sit down and negotiate with these armed gunmen,\" <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/michigan-attorney-general-far-right-aims-to-disrupt-the-state-2020-10\">Nessel told Business Insider.</a>\"That provides that cover, you know &#8212; that legitimacy. That's all they need sometimes to escalate their operations because they feel like they have the support of the president himself.\"</p>\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"Troy Balderson looks to defend his seat against Democrat Alaina Shearer in Ohio's 12th Congressional District","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/ohio-12th-district-house-election-troy-balderson-alaina-shearer-2020","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f60cda6323fc4001e0d63b1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Troy Balderson Ohio\" height=\"1104\" width=\"2208\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>12th Congressional District Republican candidate Troy Balderson speaks during a rally with President Donald Trump, Saturday, Aug. 4, 2018, in Lewis Center, Ohio.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP Photo/John Minchillo</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><strong>Rep. Troy Balderson</strong> will face Democratic challenger Alaina Shearer to represent Ohio's 12th Congressional District in the U.S. House of Representatives.</li>\n<li>The district is located in central Ohio outside of Columbus and is home to all of Delaware, Morrow, and Licking counties as well as parts of Franklin, Marion, Richland, and Muskingum counties.</li>\n<li>Balderson is finishing his first full term in office after being elected in a 2018 special election.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>After finishing his first full term, <strong>Rep. Troy Balderson</strong> looks to defend his House seat against Democratic challenger <strong>Alaina Shearer</strong>.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Balderson is a former state senator and state representative in Ohio, positions he held for 12 years in total. He was first elected to the U.S. House of Representatives in a high-profile 2018 special election held after former Rep. Pat Tiberi announced his resignation from office to lead the Ohio Business Roundtable.&#160;</p><p>In the special election, Balderson defeated Franklin County Recorder Danny O'Connor by just <a href=\"https://www.politico.com/story/2018/08/24/ohio-special-election-results-troy-balderson-795697\">0.8 percentage points</a>. He later defeated O'Connor in the 2018 midterm election by <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/elections/results/ohio-house-district-12\">4.2 percentage points</a>. In Congress, Balderson serves on the Committees on Science, Space &#38; Technology, Small Business, and Transportation &#38; Infrastructure.&#160;</p><p>Shearer, Balderson's challenger, is a former radio reporter and news anchor and winner of two Associated Press awards. She is the founder of a small business which connects women in digital media, now known as <a href=\"https://www.togetherindigital.com/\">Together Digital</a>. Shearer is <a href=\"https://www.alaina2020.com/on-the-issues/\">running her campaign on</a> growing small businesses in Ohio, supporting the passage of the Equality Act, and legalizing marijuana.</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Ohio's <a href=\"https://www.govtrack.us/congress/members/OH/12\">12th Congressional District</a> is located in the central region of the state outside of the city of Columbus, and is home to all of Delaware, Morrow, and Licking counties as well as parts of Franklin, Marion, Richland, and Muskingum counties.</p><p>For the 2016 presidential election, the 12th District voted for now-President Donald Trump over Democratic nominee Hillary Clinton by nine points in a 53-42 percentage point split of the vote, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/07/09/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\">according to Daily Kos</a>.</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=OH12&spec=Np;spec=N\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Balderson has raised $1.3 million for his campaign, spent $600,000, and currently has $755,000 on hand as the November election approaches. His opponent, Shearer, has raised about $451,000, has spent $251,000, and has about $200,000 left to spend on her campaign.</p><h2>What some of the experts say</h2><p>The race between Balderson and Shearer is rated as \"safe Republican\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a> and \"likely Republican\" by the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report</a> and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" data-show-header=\"false\">Expanded Coverage Module: REUTERS/John Vizcaino\" height=\"3768\" width=\"5664\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Marijuana plants are seen at Ganja Farms marijuana store in Bogota\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong><em>Welcome to Insider Cannabis, our weekly newsletter where we're bringing you an inside look at the deals, trends, and personalities driving the multibillion-dollar global cannabis boom.</em></strong></p><p><strong><em><a href=\"http://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/cultivated\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"87b2b2f73e32f9ba900b74923c1b176e\">Sign up here to get it in your inbox every week</a>.</em></strong></p><p>Happy Friday readers,</p><p>If you caught the VP debate this Wednesday, you probably heard Sen. Kamala Harris' comment about cannabis decriminalization. This sent stocks soaring the following morning (read Jeremy's coverage <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/marijuana-stocks-curaleaf-canopy-growth-surge-as-harris-touts-decriminalization-2020-10\">here</a>), though we shouldn't be surprised considering Harris co-sponsored the MORE Act, a bill to federally legalize cannabis and expunge criminal records, in the Senate.</p><p>It's a strong signal that if Joe Biden wins, the Democratic administration would back cannabis reform.</p><p>And cannabis reform is a major subplot of the November 3 election. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/marijuana-legalization-ballot-tracker-new-jersey-arizona-montana-vote-results-2020\">Here's everything you need to know, in a cool graphic</a>.&#160;</p><p><em>-Yeji</em></p><p><strong><em>Here's what we wrote about this week:</em></strong></p><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/marijuana-legalization-ballot-tracker-new-jersey-arizona-montana-vote-results-2020\">The ultimate guide to marijuana legalization: Here are all the states voting on cannabis reform in November, the probability of success, and which stocks could benefit the most</a></h3><p>With less than a month to go until the election,&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cannabis\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"1e3d6b719bf38fadd08239d4bdb7dd10\">cannabis</a>&#160;executives, investors, and activists are focused on five key states.</p><p>To put together this ballot tracker, we tapped a variety of sources to explain the nuances of each state's ballot measures and where polling stands. We relied on analysts from the investment bank Cowen, who generated probabilities for how likely each ballot measure is to pass.&#160;</p><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/medical-cannabis-company-columbia-care-gears-up-for-recreational-2020-10\"><strong>Medical cannabis giant Columbia Care just made a major move into recreational pot as it gears up for 'high appetite' in states poised to legalize</strong></a></h3><p>The giant medical cannabis company Columbia Care is laying the groundwork to profit from a new wave of cannabis legalization that could be on the horizon. Columbia Care, which operates in 10 states, is building on its medical-roots image by launching a national recreational brand, called Seed &#38; Strain.</p><p>The move comes less than a month before four states — New Jersey, Arizona, South Dakota, and Montana — will vote on legalizing cannabis for all adults, and amid a backdrop where cannabis brands are gearing up to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/companies-how-positioning-to-profit-more-states-make-cannabis-legal-2020-9\">build out national footprints.</a></p><h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/marijuana-stocks-curaleaf-canopy-growth-surge-as-harris-touts-decriminalization-2020-10\"><strong>Kamala Harris just said her administration will decriminalize marijuana if Biden wins, and cannabis stocks are soaring</strong></a></h3><p>Cannabis stocks soared after Sen. Kamala Harris said a Biden administration would decriminalize marijuana at the federal level. Curaleaf, Harvest Health &#38; Recreation, and Aphria are among the top gainers, though the entire sector seems to have been energized by Harris' statement at the debate.&#160;</p><h2>Deals, launches, and IPOs</h2><ul><li>Field Trip Health <a href=\"https://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/field-trip-health-ltd-to-commence-trading-on-the-cse-on-october-6-under-ticker-symbol-ftrp-301145891.html\">began trading on the Canadian Securities Exchange</a> (CSE) on Tuesday.</li><li>Psychedelics company MindMed <a href=\"https://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/mindmed-partners-with-nyu-langone-medical-center-to-launch-groundbreaking-training-program-for-psychedelic-therapies-and-medicines-301145393.html\">partnered with NYU</a> to establish a Center for Psychedelic Medicine at NYU Langone Health.</li><li>Subversive Capital, a cannabis real estate SPAC, <a href=\"https://www.newswire.ca/news-releases/subversive-real-estate-acquisition-reit-lp-announces-us-182-8-million-qualifying-transaction-to-become-publicly-traded-internally-managed-cannabis-reit-881444514.html\">announced it acquired $182.8 million of industrial cannabis properties</a> in California, Florida, Ohio and other states. The deal converts Subversive from a SPAC (known as de-SPACing) into a publicly-traded cannabis REIT.</li><li>Pabst Labs launched the <a href=\"https://www.cannabisbusinesstimes.com/article/pabst-blue-ribbon-cannabis-infused-seltzer-debuts-in-california/\">Pabst Blue Ribbon THC-infused seltzer</a> in select dispensaries in California. Pabst Labs was founded by a group from the eponymous beer company, which licensed out its name for the cannabis beverage.&#160;</li><li>Cannabis company <a href=\"https://www.globenewswire.com/news-release/2020/10/06/2104244/0/en/Stem-Holdings-Inc-Announces-Signing-of-Definitive-Agreement-to-Acquire-Driven-Deliveries-Inc-Stem-Holdings-will-become-Driven-By-Stem.html#:~:text=Stem%20Holdings%2C%20Inc.-,Announces%20Signing%20of%20Definitive%20Agreement%20to%20Acquire%20Driven%20Deliveries%2C%20Inc,will%20become%20Driven%20By%20Stem&text=The%20acquisition%20(the%20%E2%80%9CAcquisition%E2%80%9D,)%20by%20Stem%20Holdings%2C%20Inc.&text=The%20Acquisition%20is%20expected%20to,as%20an%20all%2Dstock%20transaction.saction.\">Stem Holdings is merging with Driven Deliveries Inc</a>. The all-stock transaction is expected to close before the end of 2020, giving the newly combined company a value of $54 million.&#160;</li><li>Guitarist Carlos Santana is <a href=\"https://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/carlos-santana-launches-new-cannabis-brand-mirayo-inspired-by-latin-heritage-301146136.html\">launching a cannabis brand in California</a>, Mirayo by Santana, in partnership with Left Coast Ventures.&#160;</li><li>Canadian cannabis company MediPharm Labs <a href=\"http://www.globenewswire.com/news-release/2020/10/05/2103325/0/en/European-Pharmaceutical-Company-STADA-Enters-Exclusive-Medical-Cannabis-Partnership-with-MediPharm-Labs.html\">entered into a supply agreement</a> with Bain Capital-backed German pharma company STADA. The deal will eventually allow MediPharm to ship its cannabis in Germany and across all of STADA's markets, where laws allow.&#160;</li></ul><h2>Policy Moves</h2><ul><li>Illinois Governor J.B. Pritzker, who has already pardoned over 11,000 individuals for cannabis-related offenses, said on Tuesday that <a href=\"https://www.marijuanamoment.net/illinois-governor-to-pardon-more-people-for-marijuana-in-the-coming-months/\">he plans to pardon more individuals in the coming months</a> as part of a larger effort to create a \"more equitable criminal justice system.\"</li><li>Vermont Gov. Phil Scott said on Wednesday that the state will finally allow recreational marijuana sales, by allowing a bill passed by Vermont's legislature to take effect without his signature. Vermont legalized cannabis in 2018 for adults over the age of 21 but did not specifically allow commercial sales within the state.&#160;</li><li>In other Northeast cannabis news, <a href=\"https://www.pressherald.com/2020/10/09/handful-of-stores-open-on-maine-cannabis-markets-inaugural-day/\">recreational cannabis sales officially began</a> on Friday morning in Maine after the state legalized marijuana in 2016.&#160;</li></ul><h2>Research and reform</h2><ul><li>Using cannabis before surgery could increase pain, require more anesthesia, and complicate recovery, according to research presented at the annual meeting of the American Society of Anesthesiologists on Monday. The researchers say it's important to let your doctors know if you have used cannabis prior to undergoing a procedure so they can adjust accordingly and that more research is needed.&#160;</li></ul><h2>Chart of the week</h2><p>In the second quarter of 2020, cannabis prices on Ontario's Cannabis Store (OCS) beat out flower prices on the illicit market for the first time. The drop in prices comes in conjunction with a growing market takeover from the legal market: OCS says that in Q2, legal sales made up 25.1% of the total market, compared to 24.7% in Q1.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f7f413a282c500018c79651?format=jpeg\" alt=\"The price of legal pot is dropping in Ontario\" height=\"840\" width=\"1240\" 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"Jaime Herrera Beutler faces a rematch against Carolyn Long in Washington's 3rd Congressional district","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/washington-3rd-district-house-election-jaime-herrera-beutler-carolyn-long-2020","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f53f5c5e6ff30001d4e750f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Carolyn Long \" height=\"1000\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>In this Aug. 22, 2018 file photo, Carolyn Long, a Democratic candidate in the 3rd Congressional District race, stands in front of her campaign office as she poses for a photo in Vancouver, Wash.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP Photo/Rachel La Corte, File</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>\n<p>Rep. <strong>Jaime Herrera Beutler&#160;</strong>and Democrat&#160;<strong>Carolyn Long&#160;</strong>are facing a rematch in Washington's 3rd Congressional District.&#160;</p>\n</li>\n<li>Herrera Beutler, seeking a fifth term to Congress, is the only Latina Republican woman with voting power in the House.&#160;</li>\n<li>Washington's 3rd District occupies a mix of cities and rural areas in the southwestern part of the state bordering Oregon. The district voted for Mitt Romney in 2012 and President Trump in 2016.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>GOP Rep.&#160;<strong>Jaime Herrera Beutler&#160;</strong>and Democrat&#160;<strong>Carolyn Long&#160;</strong>are facing a rematch in Washington's 3rd Congressional District.&#160;</p><h2>The candidates:</h2><p>Herrera Beutler has served in Congress representing Southwest Washington since 2011, and is now seeking a fifth term.</p><p>A former member of the Washington state legislature, she's one of just 11 Republican female representatives running for re-election in 2020, and is the only Latina Republican woman with voting power in the House. She and Rep. Don Young of Alaska are the only House Republicans to represent the Pacific Coastline.&#160;</p><p>In Congress, Herrera Beutler has positioned herself as a relatively centrist, business-friendly Republican. She serves on the powerful House Appropriations Committee and on the US Joint Economic Committee.&#160;</p><p>\"Herrera Beutler's profile — female, Hispanic and one of a dwindling number of Republican representatives from the West Coast — makes her a precious asset for the GOP, which has seen its female ranks in the House slashed by almost half since 2011,\" <a href=\"https://www.politico.com/news/magazine/2019/12/11/can-the-republican-party-save-its-only-latina-voting-congresswoman-076693\">Politico Magazine wrote in December 2019.</a></p><p>The congresswoman has largely voted along the party lines, but has not closely attached herself to President Donald Trump nor embraced his brand of politics as readily as many of her Republican colleagues in the House.&#160;</p><p>\"My goal is not to be (Trump's) foil, but it's not to be his loyal servant,\" she told Politico Magazine in 2019. \"To the degree that he is serving the people I represent, I'm there, I'm with him. To the degree that there's a problem, I'll oppose him.\"</p><p>Long, her Democratic opponent again in 2020, is a tenured professor in the School of Politics, Philosophy and Public Affairs at Washington State University-Vancouver, focusing on American institutions and the constitution.</p><p>Her <a href=\"https://electlong.com/issues/\">campaign platform</a> emphasizes expanding affordable healthcare and bringing down prescription drug costs, enacting fairer taxes, and extending rural broadband access to rural Washington.&#160;&#160;</p><p>Herrera Beutler faced the closest reelection bid of her career against Long in 2018, defeating Long by five points, 52.7% to 47.3%.</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Washington's 3rd District occupies a swath of land in the southern part of the state bordering Oregon, stretching from the Pacific Coast towns of Tokeland and Long Beach and then inland to include the cities of Vancouver, Longview, and Goldendale.&#160;&#160;</p><p>The district, formerly a hotbed for logging and the lumber trade, includes a mix of urban and rural communities.&#160;</p><p>It has traditionally voted Republican in recent elections. In 2012, Republican presidential nominee Mitt Romney carried the district by two points, 50% to 48%, over former President Barack Obama while Trump won the district by eight points, 50% to 42%, in 2016, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2012/11/19/1163009/-Daily-Kos-Elections-presidential-results-by-congressional-district-for-the-2012-2008-elections\">according to Daily Kos Elections.&#160;</a></p><h2>The money race</h2><p>Herrera Beutler has raised $2.9 million, spent $1 million, and has $1.9 million in cash on hand, according to <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=WA03WA03\">the Center for Responsive Politics.</a> Long, by comparison, has raised $2.3 million, spent nearly $750,000, and has $1.6 million in cash on hand.&#160;</p><h2>What some of the experts say&#160;</h2><p><a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">The Cook Political Report</a>, <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>, and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball at the University of Virginia Center for Politics</a> all rate this race as \"likely Republican.\"&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"The best budget binoculars","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-budget-binoculars","description":"<ul class=\"summary-list\"><li><strong>Many binoculars are expensive, but a great pair of binoculars doesn't have to cost a fortune. In fact, there are many good picks under $120, with many priced far below that. </strong></li><li><strong>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00B7LQARS/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B00B7LQARS&linkId=6ee65841809cb128d600e98ba67b3c68809cb128d600e98ba67b3c68\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Nikon 8248 ACULON A211 10x50 Binocular</a> is our top budget pick because it's versatile, lightweight, and doesn't skimp on image quality.</strong></li></ul><p>Finding the right pair of binoculars starts with a purpose.</p><p>You might be looking for the best binoculars for birding, in which case, you'll want something lightweight and compact to hold for an extended period of time. Something for astronomy will be heavier, as you'll want higher magnification to see farther into the night sky. Or, maybe you're looking to pick up an affordable pair for kids.&#160;</p><p>Of course, the price also comes into play. While having a budget in mind is definitely helpful, many options are less expensive than you think, and a low price doesn't mean binoculars will be strictly barebones. Some come with neck straps and carrying pouches, others let you attach a smartphone to shoot photos or videos.&#160;</p><p>And, many top picks are around $100 or less. We researched some of the best binoculars on a budget and compiled the following list to help meet your needs. Of course, these are not professional-level binoculars, but they will suit hobbyists and casual users just fine.&#160;</p><h2>Here are the best budget binoculars:</h2><ul class=\"summary-list\"><li><strong>Best overall: <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00B7LQARS/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B00B7LQARS&linkId=6ee65841809cb128d600e98ba67b3c68809cb128d600e98ba67b3c68\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Nikon Aculon A211 10 x 50 Binoculars</a></strong></li><li><strong>Best value: <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07HKLFCQD/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B07HKLFCQD&linkId=2930462b4c89c792ac05ebd075d2afef4c89c792ac05ebd075d2afef\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">ZoomX X-007 Binoculars with Smartphone Adapter</a></strong></li><li><strong>Best under $40: <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00004TBLW/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B00004TBLW&linkId=5b2321f85d4e4cfdd71d8a04c39139705d4e4cfdd71d8a04c3913970\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Bushnell Falcon 133410 Binoculars</a></strong></li><li><strong>Best for kids: <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B018ZONTOQ/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B018ZONTOQ&linkId=0232bfffbab8d87f8052c7f1375fac60bab8d87f8052c7f1375fac60\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Kidwinz Shock Proof 8x21 Kids Binoculars</a></strong></li><li><strong><strong style=\"color: #000000;\">Best for astronomy: <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003AM87Q4/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B003AM87Q4&linkId=3f1ce49f3c311f5b5f2467da186d1c6f3c311f5b5f2467da186d1c6f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Celestron 71008 SkyMaster 25x70 Binoculars</a></strong></strong></li></ul><p><em>Updated on 10/9/2020 to edit prices, links, formatting, and titles.</em></p>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\tThe best overall\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ce6c1f7f85e1633704936e9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Nikon Aculon Binoculars\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00B7LQARS/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B00B7LQARS&#38;linkId=6ee65841809cb128d600e98ba67b3c68\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Nikon Aculon A211 10 x 50 binoculars</a> suit a wide range of purposes, from birding to travel and sporting events, and are lightweight enough to bring along for the day.</h3><p>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00B7LQARS/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B00B7LQARS&#38;linkId=6ee65841809cb128d600e98ba67b3c68\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Nikon Aculon A211 10x50 binoculars</a> can't be beaten for its blend of quality and affordability for the price.</p><p>These binoculars are lightweight and ergonomic, which means you can carry it around easily all day. A smooth-turning focus knob lets you quickly and accurately find a clear view of your subject. The rubberized coating provides a strong grip.</p><p>These binoculars are 10 x 50, which means 10x magnification with a 50mm objective diameter. They also have a 5mm <a href=\"https://imaging.nikon.com/lineup/sportoptics/how_to/guide/binoculars/basic/basic_05.htm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">exit pupil</a>. In short, these binoculars work just as well for birding and outdoor activities as they do for viewing the night sky. That's because 10 x 50 binoculars have a wider aperture, which is better for seeing distant objects, even at night.</p><p>In terms of the exit pupil, binoculars with <a href=\"https://binocularsguru.com/what-do-the-numbers-on-binoculars-mean/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">at least 4mm</a> are suitable for most conditions, even low light.&#160;</p><p>Weight is another big factor. These binoculars weigh <a href=\"https://www.nikonsportoptics.com/en/nikon-products//binoculars/aculon-a211-10x50.html#tab-ProductDetail-ProductTabs-TechSpecs\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">31.7 ounces</a> or approximately 2 pounds. While they're not the most lightweight binoculars out there, they'll be easy to carry around, unless you're carrying other equipment, of course.</p><p>The lenses deliver clarity and brightness, helped by a special coating that is applied. Like Nikon's cameras lenses, which Insider Picks Guides Editor Les Shu has experience with, these are high-quality optics (Nikon is renowned for its glass and build quality). The rubber eyecups keep peepers positioned at the correct point and makes the binoculars more comfortable to use over an extended period.</p><p>Unfortunately, the binoculars are not weatherproof, so you'd need to take care when using them in certain environments. But it's a tradeoff we are willing to make for a quality product at such a low price.</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Ideal for general use, ergonomic, many user-friendly features</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Long-distance images may appear wavy, not weatherproof, protective lens caps fall off easily</p>\n\tThe best value\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ce6c3c6828ac13b23498913?format=jpeg\" alt=\"ZoomX binoculars\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07HKLFCQD/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07HKLFCQD&#38;linkId=2930462b4c89c792ac05ebd075d2afef\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">ZoomX X-007 Binoculars with Smartphone Adapter</a> is waterproof and works with a smartphone to capture images and videos digitally.</h3><p>Instead of excelling in a single area, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07HKLFCQD/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07HKLFCQD&#38;linkId=2930462b4c89c792ac05ebd075d2afef\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow\">X-007 10 x 42 binoculars</a> from ZoomX are suitable for a wide range of outdoor activities, whether it is birdwatching or a game at the stadium They also use <a href=\"http://www.strathspey.co.uk/numbers.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">BAK-4 prisms</a>, which tend to be denser and transmit more light. Combined with fully multi-coated lenses, the result is optimal contrast and clear images, even when the weather is less than ideal.</p><p>Speaking of foul weather, these binoculars have an IPX 7 rating, which means they are waterproof and can be temporarily immersed in water up to approximately 5 feet. Nitrogen filling also helps reduce fogging.</p><p>Weight is also important. At <a href=\"https://www.zoomx.company/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">1.24 pounds</a>, these binoculars are lighter than our overall pick and will fit into most backpacks or carrying cases. A rubberized body prevents the binoculars from slipping out of your hand.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07HKLFCQD/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07HKLFCQD&#38;linkId=2930462b4c89c792ac05ebd075d2afef\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">X-007</a> has another feature I find really handy. Say, you have an amazing up-close look at an exotic bird, unique animal, or a memorable moment in a sporting event. Wouldn't it be great if you could capture it and share with others? With a smartphone attachment, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07HKLFCQD/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07HKLFCQD&#38;linkId=2930462b4c89c792ac05ebd075d2afef\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">X-007</a> lets you do just that.</p><p>Essentially, the mount places your phone's camera over one of the eyecups. With the 10x-magnified image on your phone's screen, you can take photos or shoot videos of what you see. The images are then stored in your camera roll, which you can share to social media. (Note: You can find similar accessories to use with other binoculars.)</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Water resistant, nitrogen filling prevents fogging, smartphone adapter</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Some find the smartphone adapter a bit awkward, neck strap isn't the best</p>\n\tThe best under $40\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ce6cde2df29c836404d7e44?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Bushnell binoculars\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Despite the name, these economical <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00004TBLW/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B00004TBLW&#38;linkId=5b2321f85d4e4cfdd71d8a04c3913970\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Bushnell Falcon 133410</a> binoculars come in handy for more than just bird watching.</h3><p>Bushnell is one of the bigger names when it comes to outdoor goods, including binoculars. This 7 x 35 model is a solid choice if you're looking for a budget pair with a decent image picture. The 1.3-pound <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00004TBLW/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B00004TBLW&#38;linkId=5b2321f85d4e4cfdd71d8a04c3913970\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">Bushnell Falcon 133410</a> has a 20-foot close-focusing distance, 12mm eye relief, and a 5mm exit pupil. <a href=\"http://www.strathspey.co.uk/numbers.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">According to Strathspey</a>, a Scottish binoculars retailer, most generally have an eye relief of 8-13mm. For best results, you'll want an optimal balance between the field of view and magnification.</p><p>Image quality doesn't have to be compromised when shopping on a budget. Aside from certain specifications, various features can enhance your viewing experience. For example, these binoculars use a <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Porro_prism\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Porro prism</a> along with coated lenses to ensure sharp image viewing. Fold-down eye cups accommodate sunglasses and eyeglasses while protecting against scratching. An instant-focus lever allows you to easily fine-tune magnification for precise feedback.</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Users can fine-tune magnification, eyecups protect lenses, comes with storage case and straps</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Not water resistant, case and straps aren't the highest quality, lens caps fall off easily</p>\n\tThe best for kids\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ce6ce95828ac13e2a47f388?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Kids binoculars\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B018ZONTOQ/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B018ZONTOQ&#38;linkId=0232bfffbab8d87f8052c7f1375fac60\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Kidwinz Shock Proof 8 x 21 Kids Binoculars</a> are durable and rugged, yet come with optics so crisp and clear, even some adults are surprised.</h3><p>Kids like to explore. However, they're also a bit more accident-prone. If you're going to buy a pair of binoculars for kids, you want one that's durable and sturdy enough to withstand outdoor adventures. <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B018ZONTOQ/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B018ZONTOQ&#38;linkId=0232bfffbab8d87f8052c7f1375fac60\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">This pair from Kidwinz</a> has a rubber coating that absorbs impact. The eyepieces are surrounded by a rubber coating, as well, to help protect the lenses.&#160;</p><p>These binoculars stand out for more than just their rugged design, although that's certainly a big draw for kids who love the outdoors. BAK-4 (a type of Porro) prisms produce sharp images.&#160;</p><p>These 8 x 21 binoculars magnify objects up to eight times, which is plenty for kids who want to explore. They're also designed for fast and even focusing, even when used by children. For the best viewing, the binoculars can be folded to match the eye distance of the child.&#160;</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Rugged, sharp images, extra rubber coating adds durability</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Strap doesn't break away for safety, focus can be hard to adjust</p>\n\tThe best for astronomy\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ce6cf8ff85e1637365f110d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Celestron binoculars\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003AM87Q4/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_052319_best-binoculars-under-100-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B003AM87Q4&#38;linkId=3f1ce49f3c311f5b5f2467da186d1c6f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">These Celestron binoculars</a> are well suited for watching the night sky, with their Porro prism optics, large objective lenses, and easy-to-focus knob.</h3><p>Even the best astronomy binoculars can't match the optics of a telescope, but that doesn't mean you can't enjoy clear views of celestial objects such as planets and stars.</p><p>These 25 x 70 binoculars have enhanced magnification and larger objective lenses. <a href=\"https://skytechlasers.com/binoculars-for-astronomy/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">According to Skytech Lasers</a>, the larger the objective lens, the brighter the image. That's because larger lenses can draw in more light.</p><p>Magnification is also key for proper viewing. While some binoculars start at 10x, images appear even larger with 25x magnification, naturally. When it comes to specifications, some astronomers want to know all the details. These binoculars have a linear field of view of 141 feet (47 meters) and a 2.8mm exit pupil. There's also 13mm eye relief and a 75-foot close focus.</p><p>An <a href=\"https://garyseronik.com/understanding-binocular-exit-pupils/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">article</a> by Gary Seronik, an astronomy expert, explores the advantages of smaller exit pupils in more powerful binoculars such as these. Smaller exit pupils, such as the 2.8mm in these binoculars, results in a darker sky background and enhanced contrast among stars.</p><p>While these binoculars are designed to be versatile, you're probably going to spend the majority of your time looking up at the sky. That's one reason why many astronomers are willing to put up with the relatively hefty <a href=\"https://www.celestron.com/products/skymaster-25x70-binocular\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">3.25-pound weight</a>. Such an intense magnification also essentially requires a tripod to ensure images are as still as possible.</p><p>Additionally, adjusting these binoculars may not be the most intuitive or fastest process.</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Ideal for sky and land viewing, long eye-relief ideal for those who wear glasses, powerful magnification</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Needs a tripod for stable images, heavy, focusing can be tedious</p>\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/best-budget-binoculars'>Business stars","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/michelin-reviews-burger-king-after-the-chain-requested-star-rating-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f8086ae4c3b2e0019bba26b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Burger King whopper meal 24\" height=\"1357\" width=\"1809\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Irene Jiang / Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Reviewers inspected Burger King restaurants in Luxembourg and Belgium to see whether its new Master Angus burger deserves a Michelin stars.</li>\n<li>They treated the fast-food chain like any other restaurant they review, and remained anonymous during their visit.</li>\n<li>Burger King has to wait until November 1 to hear the verdict.</li>\n<li>Last month, Burger King Belgium launched a petition to get a Michelin star for the restaurant's new Master Angus burger, telling reviewers: \"yes, you will be served on a tray.\"</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Two Michelin reviewers visited two Burger King restaurants in Luxembourg and Belgium to see whether the fast-food chain deserves one of its coveted stars.</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The inspectors both ordered a full meal, including Burger King's Master Angus burger, Michelin told Business Insider. The reviewers remained anonymous during their visit to ensure staff didn't give them preferential treatment.</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The inspectors then drew up a report based on the five criteria of the Michelin Guide: product quality; mastery of cooking techniques; the personality of the chef in their cuisine; harmony of flavors; and consistency between visits.</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><em><strong>See more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-burger-king-chipotle-dominos-and-subway-market-in-pandemic-2020-4\">Here's how Burger King, Chipotle, Domino's, and Subway are adapting their marketing as customers move to a delivery-based future</a></em></p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The two inspectors will meet to discuss their visits and decide whether to award a star to Burger King.</p><p style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But the chain will have to wait until November 1 to see whether Michelin has included it in its next guide for Belgium &#38; Luxembourg.</p><h2>\"You will be served on a tray,\" says Burger King</h2><p>The Michelin inspection comes after Burger King in Belgium and Luxembourg <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/burger-king-belgium-launches-petition-for-burger-michelin-star-2020-10\">launched a Change.org petition last month to get a Michelin star for its new Master Angus burger.</a></p><p>\"We know very well that 'Burger King' and 'Michelin star restaurant' don't mix,\" Burger King Belgium CEO Kevin Derycke wrote on the petition.</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;Burger King Belgium Gaming  (@BurgerKingBE_GG) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1308844484281667590?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">September 23, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>Rather than silver cutlery, satin tablecloths, and valet parking, reviewers will be faced with paper napkins, finger dining, and a drive-thru, Burger King Belgium CEO Kevin Derycke joked.</p><p>\"And yes, you will be served on a tray,\" he told Michelin reviewers.</p><p>\"Who said you needed silver service?\" Michelin responded.</p><h2>The Michelin Guide was launched to sell tires</h2><p>The Michelin brothers, who were French car tire manufacturers, launched the Michelin Guide with maps, hotel and restaurant information, and tire repair advice in 1900. Their aim was to encourage more people to drive — and in turn, buy more tires — at a time when there were fewer than 3,000 cars in the country.</p><p>Over the decades this expanded to include a more comprehensive restaurant guide. The brothers also started to charge for the guide, and removed the paid-for advertisements previously included.</p><p>As the influence of the guide grew, the brothers recruited a team to visit and review restaurants anonymously.</p><p>The guide first awarded a single star to the highest-quality restaurants in 1926, but five years later it expanded this so that restaurants could be awarded up to three stars.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/michelin-reviews-burger-king-after-the-chain-requested-star-rating-2020-10'>Business Joyce Elliott, D-Little Rock, speaks at the Arkansas state Capitol in Little Rock, Ark. Elliott is hoping to unseat Republican U.S. Rep. French Hill in the fall election. Hill a Republican congressman in central Arkansas launched his first campaign ad Tuesday, Aug. 18, 2020, in which he touts the federal coronavirus relief the state has received.\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP Photo/Danny Johnston, File</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Republican Rep. French Hill is running for reelection against Democratic Joyce Elliot in Arkansas' 2nd District.</li>\n<li>This Central Arkansas-based district includes the state's capital of Little Rock and the surrounding counties.&#160;</li>\n<li>Elliot was recently added to the Democratic Congressional Campaign Committee's \"Red to Blue\" program which aims to assist the campaigns of top-tier candidates.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Republican&#160;<strong>Rep. French Hill&#160;</strong>is running against Democratic candidate&#160;<strong>Joyce Elliot&#160;</strong>in Arkansas' 2nd Congressional District.</p><h2>The candidates:</h2><p>Hill, a former bank CEO and economic policy adviser under the George W. Bush administration, has represented this seat since 2015 and is now seeking a fourth term in Congress. He first ran for the seat in 2014 when its previous representative Tim Griffin retired to run for Lieutenant Governor.&#160;</p><p>In Congress, Hill serves on the powerful House Financial Services Committee and is Ranking Member of the National Security, International Development, and Monetary Policy Subcommittee. He's voted in line with President Donald Trump 97% of the time since 2017, <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/congress-trump-score/french-hill/\">according to FiveThirtyEight.</a></p><p>Elliot, a native of rural Arkansas, was a public high school teacher before going into politics. She was first elected to the Arkansas state House of Representatives in 2000 and then to the State Senate in 2008, where she currently represents District 31 in Little Rock.&#160;</p><p>Her <a href=\"https://www.joyceelliott.com/policy/economy\">campaign platform</a> emphasizes expanding access to affordable healthcare and COVID-19 care in Arkansas, prioritizing economic relief for workers and businesses from the effects of COVID-19, and improving equitable education,&#160;</p><p>Recently, Elliot was added to the Democratic Congressional Campaign Committee's <a href=\"https://dccc.org/dccc-adds-joyce-elliott-dccc-red-blue-program/\">\"Red to Blue\" program for top-tier candidates</a>. Hill is far from a flamethrower or a bombastic partisan, but the DCCC <a href=\"https://dccc.org/case-congressman-french-hill/\">is painting him as a rubber stamp for Trump's agenda and the interests of big corporations.&#160;</a></p><p>In 2018, Hill defeated his Democratic opponent in the general election by a margin of six points, 52% to 46%.&#160;</p><h2>The district&#160;</h2><p>Arkansas' 2nd District includes the state's capital city of Little Rock and some of the surrounding suburbs.&#160;</p><p>This seat is located in a deep red state and the district may seem safe Republican at first glance. But as election data analyst Noah Rudnick <a href=\"https://medium.com/@rudnicknoah/the-hot-seat-2020-arkansas-2nd-district-77083972bdb7\">first argued in April</a>, demographic trends including a growing population of young families settling in the Little Rock suburbs and a steadily increasing share of nonwhite voters, could make the district more competitive for Democrats this year and beyond.&#160;</p><p>The district backed 2012 Republican presidential nominee Mitt Romney by a margin of 12 percentage points and voted for Trump in 2016 by 10 points, 52% to 42%, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2012/11/19/1163009/-Daily-Kos-Elections-presidential-results-by-congressional-district-for-the-2012-2008-elections\">according to Daily Kos Elections.&#160;</a></p><h2>The money race:</h2><p>So far, Hill has raised $1.9 million, spent nearly $500,000, and has $1.4 million in cash on hand, <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=AR02AR02\">according to the Center for Responsive Politics</a>. Elliot has raised $1 million, spent nearly $320,000, and has $719,000 in cash on hand.&#160;</p><h2>What some of the experts say:</h2><p>The race between Hill and Elliot is rated as \"leans Republican\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>, <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball at the University of Virginia Center for Politics</a>, and the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">The Cook Political Report.</a></p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" authoritarian","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/gop-sen-mike-lee-says-rank-democracy-bad-for-america-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f80a481ea74820019ca6482?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Sen. Mike Lee\" height=\"1249\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Republican Sen. Mike Lee of Utah.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Tasos Katopodis/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>GOP Sen. Mike Lee took to Twitter this week to argue that the US is \"not a democracy,\" sparking fierce backlash.</li>\n<li>Lee's statements, which mischaracterized the nature of the US political system, struck a nerve at a time when President Donald Trump is fueling divisions in the US and undermining the legitimacy of the election.</li>\n<li>\"Authoritarianism in a nutshell,\" one historian and expert on democracy said in response to Lee's tweets.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Republican Sen. Mike Lee courted controversy this week when he tweeted that \"rank democracy\" is a threat to American prosperity.</p><p>\"We're not a democracy,\" <a href=\"https://twitter.com/SenMikeLee/status/1314016169993670656?s=20\">Lee said</a>. \"Democracy isn't the objective; liberty, peace, and prosperity are. We want the human condition to flourish. Rank democracy can thwart that.\"</p><p>\"The word 'democracy' appears nowhere in the Constitution, perhaps because our form of government is not a democracy. It's a constitutional republic,\" Lee added. \"To me it matters. It should matter to anyone who worries about the excessive accumulation of power in the hands of the few.\"</p><p>The Utah Republican's tweets on the matter are linked to a long history of Republicans rejecting the notion that the US political system is a democracy. The GOP's objection to calling the US a democracy is tied to the fact Republicans have reason to fear a system in which a majority of Americans have more say. The Republican party's platform is increasingly at odds with the perspectives of most voters on an array of issues.&#160;</p><p>But Lee's portrayal of democracy as something that can hinder progress in the US could also be viewed in a more chilling light given the Republican senator is an ally of a president who has rapidly eroded democratic norms during his tenure and is actively working to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-is-trying-to-undermine-legitimacy-of-the-2020-election-2020-7\">undermine the legitimacy of the 2020 election</a>.</p><p>President Donald Trump has refused to commit to a peaceful transfer of power, for example, and has essentially <a href=\"https://www.politico.com/news/2020/10/07/trump-demands-barr-arrest-foes-427389\">called for his political rivals to be jailed.</a> The president has baselessly claimed that the election is \"rigged\" against him as he trails former Vice President Joe Biden in the polls. Trump's behavior has <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/historians-election-experts-warn-trump-behaving-like-mussolini-2020-9?utmSource=twitter&utmContent=referral&utmTerm=topbar&referrer=twitterrrer=twitter\">mirrored that of authoritarians</a>, and alarmed historians and scholars of democracy.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f80a3444c3b2e0019bba371?format=jpeg\" alt=\"trump day US President Donald Trump departs a rally at Dayton International Airport in Dayton, Ohio September 21, 2020. (Photo by MANDEL NGAN / AFP) (Photo by MANDEL NGAN/AFP via Getty Images)\" height=\"680\" width=\"907\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Mandel Ngan/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Lee's tweets on democracy, which began on Wednesday and <a href=\"https://twitter.com/SenMikeLee/status/1314089207875371008?s=20\">carried into Thursday</a>, struck a nerve with many people at a time when experts have warned that American democracy is in mortal danger.</p><p>Walter Shaub, former director of the US office of government ethics,&#160;<a href=\"https://twitter.com/waltshaub/status/1314186836839993345\" data-link-name=\"in body link\">said</a>: \"People of my grandfather's generation knew what to do about fascists. Now a member of Congress is urging us to join them. I wonder what made you hate America so much.\"</p><p>\"Every despot in the world has promised liberty, peace, and prosperity,\" Brian Klaas, Brian Klaas, a political scientist at the University College London, <a href=\"https://twitter.com/brianklaas/status/1314192852398858241?s=20\">said</a> via Twitter in response to Lee. \"The problem is that without democracy, you can't get rid of them when they don't actually deliver. And then you're stuck with a dictator who provides none of the above.\"</p><p>The Utah senator, who was democratically elected to the Senate in 2011, was echoing an oft-repeated line from US conservatives that <a href=\"https://www.heritage.org/american-founders/report/america-republic-not-democracy\">\"the US is a republic, not a democracy.\"</a>&#160;</p><p>This is a misleading slogan. The US is not a direct democracy, in which citizens play a direct role in voting on policy or laws, but it is a representative democracy, in which representatives are elected by citizens to be their voice in government. It is also a constitutional democracy, in which the Constitution provides for a system of checks and balances (co-equal branches of government) and therefore presents restraints on the majority.&#160;</p><p>Technically, the US is a constitutional republic. But a republic is, by definition, a type of democracy.</p><p>\"Both democracy and republic have more than a single meaning, and one of the definitions we provide for democracy closely resembles the definition of republic,\" <a href=\"https://www.merriam-webster.com/dictionary/republic\">according to Merriam-Webster</a>, which defines a republic as \"a government in which the supreme power is vested in the people and exercised by them directly or indirectly through a system of representation usually involving periodically held free elections.\"</p><p>In other words, the US is both a republic AND a democracy.</p><p>Lee painted a false dichotomy and he could not have done it at a worse moment, as many in the US feel that <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/2020/09/21/supreme-court-fight-highlights-new-political-reality-america-under-minority-rule/\">the GOP has already instituted minority rule</a> and democracy watchdogs warn that <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2020/09/18/united-states-is-backsliding-into-autocracy-under-trump-scholars-warn/\">America is becoming increasingly autocratic under Trump.</a></p><p>\"Authoritarianism in a nutshell,\" Ruth Ben-Ghiat, a historian and expert on authoritarianism at New York University, <a href=\"https://twitter.com/ruthbenghiat/status/1314217006682402817?s=20\">said</a> in response to Lee. \"Same words said from Mussolini to Orbán. GOP has judged the time right to come out and say it.\"</p><p>\"The escalation of GOP and WH rhetoric about protestors being a mob and Dems being 'too dangerous to rule' is very serious,\" <a href=\"https://twitter.com/ruthbenghiat/status/1048964002167095296?s=20\">Ben-Ghiat said</a>, warning that such talk \"often precedes\" authoritarian government actions.</p><p>Like many congressional Republicans, Lee went from being a fierce critic of Trump during the 2016 campaign season to an ally after the former reality TV star won the election. Back in 2016, Lee questioned whether Trump would be an authoritarian if elected.&#160;</p><p>\"I would like some assurances that he is going to be a vigorous defender of the U.S. Constitution, that he is not going to be an autocrat, that he is not going to be an authoritarian,\" <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2016/07/01/us/politics/mike-lee-donald-trump.html\">Lee said</a> at the time. \"That is not an unreasonable demand.\"</p><p>Fast-forward to 2020 and Lee is at the forefront of GOP efforts to confirm Trump's Supreme Court nominee prior to the election, despite the fact polling has shown a majority of Americans believe that seat should remain vacant until after Election Day.&#160;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"How to calibrate your Google Maps app to give more accurate directions, on iPhone or Android","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-calibrate-google-maps","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d8b6faa2e22af2c1c3c7089?format=jpeg\" alt=\"google maps phone\" height=\"1845\" width=\"2460\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can calibrate your Google Maps app in several ways on iPhone or Android.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><strong>You can calibrate your Google Maps app on an iPhone or Android to get better and more accurate directions.</strong></li>\n<li><strong>To calibrate Google Maps on an Android, you'll need to calibrate the compass or turn on \"high-accuracy mode.\"</strong></li>\n<li><strong>On an iPhone, make sure that both Wi-Fi and Location Services are enabled.</strong></li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>When it comes to getting directions, accuracy is everything. So when your GPS is having a hard time identifying your location, things can get frustrating — fast.&#160;</p><p>If you use <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/google-maps\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Google Maps</a>, there are ways to improve the accuracy: calibrating the compass so it points in the correct direction, for instance, or turning on high-accuracy mode on your Android phone.&#160;</p><p>There are several ways to get better directions and results while using the Google Maps app on your Android&#160;phone, as we detail below.&#160;&#160;</p><p>If you have an iPhone, however, the below methods won't work, so you should try restarting your phone or enabling Wi-Fi to improve the accuracy of your Google Maps app.</p><h2>How to calibrate Google Maps with settings on an Android phone</h2><h3>Compass calibration</h3><p>If you open your Google Maps app and see that the blue dot is pointing in the wrong direction, or is in the wrong location, calibration can help you get a more accurate reading. Here's how to do it on an Android&#160;phone:</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Go into your Google Maps app, if it's not already open.</p><p><strong>2. </strong>While holding your phone, move your hand in a figure eight motion — you should see the beam narrow as you go. Keep in mind it may take a few times for this to work.</p><h3>Turning on high-accuracy mode</h3><p>High-accuracy mode is a helpful tool in getting your Google Maps app up to speed. But keep in mind that this method only works if you have an Android:</p><p><strong>3. </strong>Open your device's Settings app.</p><p><strong>4. </strong>Tap \"Location.\" Depending on your device, it may also be labeled as \"Security and Location\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d8a82012e22af17431bc025?format=jpeg\" alt=\"2 HOW TO CALIBRATE GOOGLE MAPS\" height=\"1920\" width=\"1080\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Open your device&#39;s &#34;Location&#34; menu.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Devon Delfino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>5. </strong>Switch on the location setting, if necessary.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d8a822b2e22af166b3c1b46?format=jpeg\" alt=\"3 HOW TO CALIBRATE GOOGLE MAPS\" height=\"1920\" width=\"1080\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Make sure that location services are turned on.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Devon Delfino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>6. </strong>Tap \"Mode.\"</p><p><strong>7. </strong>Select \"High Accuracy.\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d8a824d2e22af17431bc028?format=jpeg\" alt=\"4 HOW TO CALIBRATE GOOGLE MAPS\" height=\"1920\" width=\"1080\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Activate the highest accuracy location mode.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Devon Delfino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>How to calibrate Google Maps on an iPhone or Android with other basic fixes</h2><p>There aren't as many fancy tricks to fix Google Maps on an iPhone.</p><p>First, you should turn on Wi-Fi on your phone. You don't need to connect to a network, you just need to turn on the setting. On both iPhone and Android, turning on Wi-Fi will make Google Maps more accurate, as it scans nearby Wi-Fi signals to locate you.</p><p>If that doesn't work, try restarting your iPhone or Android. Your phone's GPS sensors may simply need to be rebooted. For more information on how to restart an iPhone, see our article, \"<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-restart-iphone-7-8-x-xs-xr\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">How to restart and force-restart any iPhone model</a>.\"</p><p>Finally, on an iPhone specifically, make sure that location services are turned on. To do this:</p><p><strong>1.</strong> Open your Settings app and go to the \"Privacy\" tab.</p><p><strong>2. </strong>At the top of the Privacy screen, tap \"Location Services.\"</p><p><strong>3.&#160;</strong>Make sure that the switch at the top of the next screen is flipped to the right, and is colored green. If it's not, tap it.</p><p><strong>4.</strong> Scroll down to your list of apps until you find Google Maps, and tap on it.</p><p><strong>5.</strong> On the next screen, select either \"While Using the App\" or \"Always.\" This will allow the Google Maps app to access your precise location faster.</p><h2><strong>Related coverage from&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" Now, Straubel has his own venture and CEO title at Redwood Materials, where he <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/jb-straubel-is-building-redwood-to-recycle-old-ev-batteries-2020-10\">wants to chase the big money</a> in recycling old EV batteries.&#160;</p><p>\"A huge missing piece of the remanufacturing economy is how all the batteries and materials get unmanufactured and are looped back into the supply chain,\" he told us. \"It could be a massive, massive industry.\"</p><h2>Rivian offers six-figure salaries amid a rising talent war</h2><p>So many electric vehicle startups, not so many engineers to make them all go. The war for talent in a burgeoning space is on, and we pulled the data to get a look at <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/rivian-salaries-revealed-from-engineer-to-financial-analyst-2020-10\">how much Rivian pays its employees</a>, from engineers to financial analysts. It's no surprise that six figures is the norm.</p><h2>A startup run by a 25-year-old CEO is proving Elon Musk wrong by bringing lidar to the mass market</h2><p>Musk may have an uncanny ability to predict (and deliver) the future, but when it comes to lidar, Austin Russell thinks the Tesla CEO&#160;has it wrong. In an interview, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/luminar-elon-musk-austin-russell-lidar-volvo-cars-2020-10\">Russell explained the key moves he's made to realize that goal</a>.</p><h2>Everything else:&#160;</h2><ul><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tesla-model-y-roof-fell-off-family-claims-quality-control-concern-2020-10\">California family says the
