03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"TikTok will be around until at least after the presidential election. Here's what that means for the app's future.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/tiktok-ban-injunction-court-hearing-after-election-day-donald-trump-2020-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f40184489aff80028ab7424?format=jpeg\" alt=\"donald trump tiktok lawsuit 4x3\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2400\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Jim Watson/AFP via Getty Images; Samantha Lee/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A US federal judge has scheduled a hearing for November 4 to next decide on whether to temporarily block the US government's attempt to ban TikTok nationwide.</li>\n<li>The hearing date means TikTok's fate is secured until at least after the presidential election on November 3.</li>\n<li>Although the delay doesn't decide TikTok's future, it means that TikTok and ByteDance now have more than a month to weed through political tensions and deal negotiations to figure out what their next move should be in its fight against the US government.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The Trump administration's attempts to issue an unprecedented nationwide ban on TikTok will be delayed until at least after Election Day 2020.</p><p>A federal judge has scheduled a hearing for November 4, the day after the presidential election, to make a decision on whether the US government's ban of the viral video-sharing app can be implemented later in the month. The government's attempt at instating its first part of the ban is already being stymied by a temporary injunction granted last month, which the Trump administration appealed on Thursday.</p><p>But the impending calendar date is still a month away, meaning there's ample time for TikTok and its Beijing-based owner ByteDance to make further moves to ensure the app's future in the US. The delay gives TikTok even further leeway as it grapples to survive in a months-long battle characterized by political jockeying and back-and-forth negotiations.</p><p>But come November 4, a federal judge will be tasked with deciding whether to block the US government's planned ban, which would take place on November 12 without obstruction. The next phase of the two-part TikTok ban intends to be a complete ban, targeting internet hosting services and content delivery networks.</p><p>Holding the hearing after November 3 is significant because the election's outcome could change how ByteDance or the Trump administration approach their arguments. But the winner of the 2020 presidential election won't be sworn in until Jan. 20, and a winner <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/america-likely-wont-know-presidential-race-winner-on-election-night-2020-5\">may not be known</a> until several days after the election, meaning the judge presiding over the TikTok case will still have to make a decision on the Nov. 12 injunction.</p><p>The future looks bright for TikTok, however. TikTok already saw the court rule in its favor when it temporarily blocked the Trump administration's first executive order to stop new downloads and software updates of the app on September 27. In the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tiktok-ban-injunction-federal-judge-says-donald-trump-exceeds-ieepa-2020-9\">decision to grant the injunction</a>, US Judge Carl Nichols called into question the government's authority to issue such a ban, writing that the TikTok ban \"likely exceeds\" the administration's \"lawful bounds.\"</p><p>It remains unclear what will happen to the US government's planned TikTok ban if a deal to settle the company's ownership in the US — in the works for months, as it hits snags and pushback — is finalized. The current proposal would break off TikTok's global business into a new US-based company, in which Oracle, Walmart and US investors would have substantial stakes. However, there's still disagreement over whether the deal would give majority ownership to US investors, or whether TikTok's China-based parent company ByteDance would maintain its majority ownership.</p><p>The calls from Donald Trump and government officials to push for a ban of TikTok over its ties with China have been mounting for months. Nonetheless, the company has managed to remain in the US virtually unscathed and more popular than ever among users, despite facing a deluge of the US government's executive orders, national-security concerns, and forced sale attempts.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Ron Kind, D-Wis., arrives for a meeting of the House Democratic Caucus in the Capitol on November 15, 2018.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Tom Williams/CQ Roll Call/Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Democratic Rep. Ron Kind will face Derrick Van Orden in Wisconsin's 3rd Congressional District.</li>\n<li>The district is located in southwestern Wisconsin along the state's border with Iowa, Illinois, and Minnesota.</li>\n<li>Van Orden was spurred to run for office after Rep. Kind voted for the impeachment of President Donald Trump.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Twelve-term incumbent <strong>Rep. Ron Kind</strong> looks to defend his House seat against Republican challenger <strong>Derrick Van Orden</strong> in Wisconsin's 3rd Congressional District.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Kind is an <a href=\"https://ronkind.org/about/\">attorney and former special prosecutor</a> for the La Crosse County prosecutor's office. He has held his position in the House of Representatives since 1996, now for 12 consecutive terms.</p><p>He currently sits on the House Committee on Ways and Means, and previously sat in the Natural Resources Committee for 14 years. Kind's <a href=\"https://ronkind.org/issues/\">2020 campaign platform</a> is centered around providing affordable healthcare to Americans, restoring fiscal accountability in Congress, and lowering the costs of education.&#160;</p><p>Kind is currently chairman of the House New Democrat Coalition, a group of moderate Democrats that support fiscally responsible policies and bipartisanship in Congress, and voted against Rep. Nancy Pelosi's bid for Speaker of the House in 2019.&#160;</p><p>Van Orden is a military veteran and Navy SEAL of 26 years. Since retiring from the military, Van Orden has spent time acting and writing a book about his experiences in the military. He was <a href=\"https://www.breitbart.com/radio/2020/04/12/derrick-van-orden-ron-kinds-duplicitous-track-record-inspired-run-congress/\">inspired to run</a> for office after Rep. Kind voted for President Donald Trump's impeachment in December 2016.&#160;</p><p>Van Orden's <a href=\"https://vanordenforcongress.com/the-issues/\">campaign platform is focused on</a> rebuilding Wisconsin's economy, fully funding police forces, and protecting farming and agricultural communities in Wisconsin and around the country.&#160;</p><h2>The district</h2><p>Wisconsin's 3rd Congressional District is located in the southwestern region of the state along its border with Minnesota, Iowa, and Illinois. The 3rd District most notably includes the cities of La Crosse, Eau Claire, and much of the Wisconsin-side of the Minneapolis-St. Paul metropolitan region.</p><p>The district is also home to the counties of Adams, Buffalo, Crawford, Dunn, Eau Claire, Grant, La Crosse, Pepin, Pierce, Portage, Trempealeau, and Vernon as well as portions of Chippewa, Jackson, Juneau, Monroe, Richland, and Wood counties.</p><p>The 3rd District flipped from voting for former President Barack Obama by 11 points over GOP presidential nominee Mitt Romney in 2012 to backing Trump over Democratic nominee Hillary Clinton by four points in a 49-45 percentage point split of the vote, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/07/09/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\">according to Daily Kos</a>.</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>According to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=WI03&spec=Np;spec=N\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>, Kind has raised $1.6 million, more than double than Van Orden with $707,000. Kind also has a substantial cash on hand advantage over his challenger. He has over $3 million left to spend as the November election approaches, or over ten times more than Van Orden's $288,000.</p><h2>What some of the experts say</h2><p>The race between Kind and Van Orden is rated as \"safe Democratic\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>, \"likely Democratic\" by <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics, and \"leans Democratic\" by the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report.</a></p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" Non-audiophile wired headphones have some great things to offer, too — namely the fact that they're generally quite a bit cheaper than their wireless counterparts.&#160;</p><p>The limited edition blue version of Audio-Technica's ATH-M50x headphones were on sale for $99 on Prime Day last year. Meanwhile, the SteelSeries Arctis 7 was marked down to $100. We're hoping for similar discounts on these models and other gaming headsets once Prime Day kicks off on October 13.</p><div id=\"ProductCard_5dc0552c2f364a711070d653\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5dc0552c2f364a711070d653&type=medium&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><div id=\"ProductCard_5dd85bf5fd9db2594118af54\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: 100%\"><iframe src=\"https://produktor.businessinsider.com/productCardService?id=5dd85bf5fd9db2594118af54&type=medium&live=true\" width=\"100%\" height=\"150%\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"position:absolute; top:0; left: 0\"></iframe></div><h2>How to shop for headphones</h2><p>Headphones are available in different sizes and styles to meet different performance needs and price points. Some buyers might prefer a model that emphasizes accurate sound quality, while others may opt for a pair that prioritizes portability.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-over-ear-headphones\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Over-ear headphones</a> are larger than other styles and feature earcups that cover your ears to create a seal. This style of headphone is a good fit for people who want the best audio performance and noise isolation. On-ear headphones are similar, but their earcups simply rest on your ear rather than create a seal over them. This allows on-ear models to be a bit more compact, but they're less ideal for blocking outside noise. Gaming headsets can be either over-ear or on-ear, but they usually add an integrated boom microphone for online voice chat.</p><p>Meanwhile, if portability is your main priority, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-earbuds\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">earbuds</a> are the best option since they feature separate buds designed to rest just outside or within your ear canal. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-wireless-earbuds\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">True wireless models</a> are even more convenient since they're completely free from cables.&#160;</p><p>For more headphone recommendations and deals all year long, check out our roundup of <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/headphone-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" Steve Bullock</strong>, who is running for Senate.</p><p>Cooney has <a href=\"http://governor.mt.gov/About/Lieutenant-Governor\">decades of experience</a> in Montana's political sphere, previously serving as state senator, legislator and secretary of state. He has been lieutenant governor since 2016.</p><p>The lifelong Montanan has made affordable healthcare a top priority of his campaign, hinging off of the coronavirus pandemic. Cooney pledges to lower the cost of prescription drugs and continue expanding <a href=\"https://www.mtpr.org/post/gubernatorial-candidate-mike-cooney-public-service-health-care-and-energy\">access to Medicaid</a> should he win.&#160;</p><p>His Republican challenger Gianforte's campaign centers around boosting the economy.&#160;</p><p>Gianforte, whose background is in business, became one of the <a href=\"https://www.ktvh.com/news/montana-news/gov-candidate-gianforte-releases-10-yrs-of-income-tax-returns\">state's wealthiest people</a> when software behemoth Oracle bought his tech startup for $1.8 billion in 2011, which he co-founded in the late 1990s with his wife in Bozeman, Montana.</p><p>Five years later, Gianforte unsuccessfully tried to launch his political career in a largely self-financed <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/elections/2016/results/montana-governor-bullock-gianforte\">bid against Bullock</a> for the governorship. He lost by a slim 3.8 percentage points.</p><p>Gianforte then pursued a legislative opening in 2017 and won the special election for the state's sole congressional seat after the Trump administration appointed then-Rep. Ryan Zinke as Interior Secretary.</p><p>The candidate made national headlines on the eve of his victory when he allegedly <a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/video/2017/may/25/republican-greg-gianforte-body-slams-guardian-reporter-in-montana-video\">bodyslammed a reporter</a>, which he later <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QZBoYzpV0ds\">apologized for</a> and was charged with <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/powerpost/wp/2017/05/24/republican-candidate-in-montana-race-body-slams-reporter-prompting-police-investigation/\">misdemeanor assault.&#160;</a></p><p>President Donald Trump <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2018/10/19/us/politics/trump-greg-gianforte-montana.html\">praised the congressman</a> at a rally in Montana a year later: \"Anybody that can do a body-slam,\" he said, \"that's my kind of guy.\"</p><p>Gianforte has boasted about <a href=\"https://gregformontana.com/issues/standing-with-trump/\">working with Trump</a> to cut taxes and roll back \"unnecessary burdensome regulations\" — policies he vows to implement in Montana if elected and has <a href=\"https://www.rga.org/rga-releases-new-video-career-politician-mike-cooney/\">slammed Cooney</a> as a \"career politician\" who pushes for more \"government red tape.\"</p><h3><strong>The stakes:</strong></h3><p>The 2020 gubernatorial contests are unlike recent election cycles considering the ongoing public health crisis. Eight out of the 11 races feature <a href=\"https://fivethirtyeight.com/features/2020-governors-races-update/\">incumbents seeking reelection</a>, who may have their fates decided based on their respective coronavirus responses. Still, some safe predictions have been casted, for example, Washington state will go blue and North Dakota will go red.</p><p>Montana, however, is a slightly different ballgame: the race is open, the competition is decidedly close and voters historically do not plainly side with one party over the other.&#160;</p><p>Montana went to Trump in 2016 and has voted Republican in the past five presidential elections. The state's legislature is also GOP-controlled. Yet Democrats have held the state's highest office since 2005, and the elections have been won by narrow margins.&#160;</p><p>A Gianforte victory over Cooney would bolster Republicans nationally, and would tip the party's currently held 26 out of 50 governorships further in its favor.&#160;</p><p>Other major elections in Montana include the open US House race between <strong>Democrat Kathleen Williams</strong> and Republican State Auditor <strong>Matt Rosendale</strong> and the Senate race between Gov. Steve Bullock and incumbent <strong>Republican Steve Daines</strong>.&#160;</p><p><strong>The money race: </strong>Gianforte <a href=\"https://apps.montanafreepress.org/montana-2020/races/Governor\">has the lead</a> with roughly $4 million raised, with over $1.5 million in self-financing as of June 15. Cooney raked in $1.1 million during the same period.</p><p><strong>What the polls say: </strong>The <a href=\"https://www.realclearpolitics.com/epolls/2020/governor/mt/montana_governor_gianforte_vs_cooney-7203.html\">latest polls</a> depict Gianforte ahead of Cooney, though the contest remains close. Gianforte led by 9 percentage points in an Emerson College survey conducted July 31-Aug. 2, an uptick from a Public Policy Polling projection made earlier in July, which showed a 4-point advantage.&#160;</p><p><strong>What the experts say:</strong> The race is rated a toss-up by <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/governor-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report</a>, <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/governor\">Inside Elections</a> and <a href=\"http://crystalball.centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-governor/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia's Center for Politics.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"Rep. Tom McClintock looks to defend his House seat against Democratic challenger Brynne Kennedy in California's 4th Congressional District","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/california-4th-district-house-election-tom-mcclintock-brynne-kennedy-2020","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f5f7e07e6ff30001d4e891a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"tom mcclintock\" height=\"636\" width=\"1273\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Six-term Rep. Tom McClintock will face Democrat Brynne Kennedy in California's 4th Congressional District.&#160;</li>\n<li>The district is located in east-central California and is home to all of the counties of Alpine, Amador, Calaveras, El Dorade, Maripose, and Tuolumne.&#160;</li>\n<li>The two candidates were chosen through California's \"top-two primary\" system which places the top two candidates in the state's primary on the November ballot, regardless of party.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Six-term incumbent <strong>Rep. Tom McClintock</strong> will square off against Democratic challenger <strong>Brynne Kennedy</strong> in November in California's 4th Congressional District.</p><p>California currently has a&#160;<a href=\"https://www.sos.ca.gov/elections/primary-elections-california/\">\"top-two primary\"</a> system, meaning that the top two winners of the primary election go on the final ballot, regardless of their political party.</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>McClintock is a former California state assemblyman and state senator, positions he held for a total of 12 years. Before running for a position in the U.S. House of Representatives, McClintock ran for the office of state controller in 1994 and 1992, governor in the 2003 recall gubernatorial election, and lieutenant governor in the 2006 gubernatorial election, losing in every single one.&#160;</p><p>In Congress, McClintock serves on the House Committee on the Judiciary and the Committee on Natural Resources, focusing many of his efforts on natural resource issues important to California. McClintock has sided with President Donald Trump 88% of the time in his voting record since 2017, <a href=\"https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/congress-trump-score/tom-mcclintock/\">according to FiveThirtyEight.</a></p><p>Kennedy is a former United States gymnast and business owner of the software company Topia. She is a former columnist for the Financial Times and is the author of a book on employee mobility. Her <a href=\"https://brynneforcongress.com/issues/\">campaign is focused on</a> strengthening the Affordable Care Act, combatting wildfire threats, and modernizing the United States Department of Veterans Affairs.</p><p>In 2018, McClintock defeated Democratic challenger Jessica Morse by eight percentage points, 54% to 46%, in the general election.&#160;</p><h2>The district</h2><p>California's <a href=\"https://www.govtrack.us/congress/members/CA/4\">4th Congressional District</a> is located in an entirely inland part of east-central California, stretching down from Truckee and South Lake Tahoe in Northern California down to the area outside of Fresno.&#160;</p><p>It is home to all of the counties of Alpine, Amador, Calaveras, El Dorado, Mariposa, and Tuolumne as well as parts of Placer, Fresno, Madera, and Nevada counties. The district is home to some of California's finest scenery and natural beauty, containing the Sierra Nevada Mountains and Sequoia National Forest.</p><p>In the 2016 presidential election, the 4th District voted for Trump over Democratic candidate Hillary Clinton in a 54-39 percentage point split of the vote, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2013/7/9/1220127/-Daily-Kos-Elections-2012-election-results-by-congressional-and-legislative-districts\">according to the Daily Kos</a>.</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>Kennedy has narrowly outraised and outspent McClintock, according to the <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=CA04CA04\">Center for Responsive Politics</a>. Kennedy has brought in $1.4 million, spent $1.1 million, and has over $356,000 in cash on hand. McClintock has raised $1.35 million, spent $932,000, and currently has about $646,000 left to spend as the November election approaches.&#160;</p><h2>What experts say</h2><p>The race between McClintock and Kennedy is rated as \"safe Republican\" by <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a> and \"likely Republican\" by the <a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">Cook Political Report</a> and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball</a> at the University of Virginia Center for Politics.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" data-show-header=\"false\">Expanded Coverage Module: 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"13 books for young children that feature protagonists of color","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/kids-books-about-diversity-and-acceptance","description":"<p class=\"financial-disclaimer\"><i>When you buy through our links, we may earn money from our affiliate partners. <a href=\"https://www.insider-inc.com/commerce-on-insider-inc/\">Learn more.</a></i></p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e39b6705bc79c754b54f5b2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Diverse books for young children\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2400\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Alyssa Powell/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\"><li>Representation matters: Exposure to different people and beliefs encourages empathy, acceptance, and perspective-taking.</li><li><strong>When you encourage diversity in your children's books early, you facilitate their social-emotional intelligence.&#160;</strong></li><li><strong>Here are 13 children's books that feature protagonists of color and explore themes like empowerment, sharing, empathy, and cultural pride.</strong></li></ul><p>Undoing generations of systemic, damaging attitudes toward people of color is an enormous undertaking that is paramount to their health, safety, and quality of life. One small way you can contribute to this ongoing movement is by encouraging your children to talk and think about race. My family lives in a diverse city, but I still feel day-to-day as though we are not always exposed to or doing our most to talk about diversity or racism. This is why I make sure my children's library is full of books that feature protagonists of color, so they see and hear the things that make us similar and different.</p><p>This list includes some of the books that my children — almost 2 and 5 years old — enjoy reading. Sometimes a character's background is central to the story. Other times, it's not a focus at all.</p><p>The value of representation in your child's library is substantial. These stories frequently explore salient themes like empowerment, sharing, empathy, mental health, and cultural pride. Unlike other popular children's books, the main characters in these stories are more likely to be portrayed in STEM or leadership roles. And these books give voice to authors and illustrators of color who are <a href=\"https://blog.leeandlow.com/2018/05/10/the-diversity-gap-in-childrens-book-publishing-2018/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://blog.leeandlow.com/2018/05/10/the-diversity-gap-in-childrens-book-publishing-2018/&source=gmail&ust=1581090025731000&usg=AFQjCNFROhfPgIxA0e-m5n9fPmFBdg-_5A9fPmFBdg-_5A\">typically underrepresented in the literary world</a>. There are 11 and 5 on this list, respectively.&#160;</p><p>The books below are diverse, informative, and vividly illustrated — all the best things a picture book for children can be. Some of the titles came into our lives organically and have been enjoyed over and over. Some are new acquisitions that were thoroughly researched based on recommendations by teachers. They were all chosen because of the beauty of their characters, inside and out. If your toddler can handle non-board books, introduce these (and others like them!) as early as you can.</p>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\t\"Thank You, Omu\" by Oge Mora\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e38473d5bc79c549c2819d3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"thank you, omu\" height=\"2560\" width=\"2095\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0316431249/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0316431249&#38;linkId=353e3b489587c93692bfab8bff786eb5\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $14.99</h3><p>This is a beautifully told and illustrated story of Omu (pronounced AH-moo), who makes her best stew ever and then shares it with neighbors and friends as they drop in one by one for a taste. When there is no stew left for Omu, an impromptu feast is born, with special dishes from all of her thankful stew recipients. I love the images featured in a paper cutout style, and the way Omu's kitchen plays against the city backdrop.</p>\n\t\"Leila in Saffron\" by Rukhsanna Guidroz\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e3847125bc79c542a080a47?format=jpeg\" alt=\"leila in saffron\" height=\"1720\" width=\"1399\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"Leila in Saffron\" by Rukhsanna Guidroz available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1534425640/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=1534425640&#38;linkId=bc5d4a2bf1f93b0f446a2170d5d02fd3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $11.99</h3><p>Leila is at her grandmother's house and on the search for things that make her feel good about herself. She finds that the love of her family, the pride of cooking a good meal, and the beauty of her grandmother's saffron scarf all make her feel special. A glossary at the end helps with the pronunciation of some Arabic words woven throughout the bright colors and patterns of the story.</p>\n\t\"Mae Among the Stars\" by Roda Ahmed\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e38481a5bc79c56480584f2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"mae among the stars\" height=\"1305\" width=\"1000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"Mae Among the Stars\" by Roda Ahmed, available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0062651730/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0062651730&#38;linkId=090bbe3431093461218b2125dabd0c54\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $13.49 and <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/mae-among-the-stars-roda-ahmed/1126245573?\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $15.99</h3><p>A quiet tale about real-life astronaut Mae Jemison's early childhood challenges of asserting her desire to go to space, I love this book for its spotlight on an incredibly smart, driven woman in STEM almost as much as its message that if you \"dream it, believe it, and work hard for it, anything is possible.\" A page at the end offers a brief bio of the real Mae's lifelong achievements, solidifying that mantra as fact.</p>\n\t\"Alma and How She Got Her Name\" by Juana Martinez-Neal\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e3848ee5bc79c48b23565f2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"alma and how she got her name\" height=\"2464\" width=\"2560\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"Alma and How She Got Her Name\" by Juana Martinez-Neal, available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0763693553/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0763693553&#38;linkId=e27dba82daf6bf85f439f42c934c506f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> and <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/alma-and-how-she-got-her-name-juana-martinez-neal/1126849206?\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $15.29</h3><p>Alma doesn't love that her name has so many, well, names! But by the end of this book, she is excited to know all of the fascinating ancestors she shares them with, and it is a delight to take that journey with her. Combined with the illustrations that feel like flashbacks to the time each ancestor was alive, this is a wonderful opportunity to learn briefly about different Latinx traditions and histories.</p>\n\t\"Jabari Jumps\" by Gaia Cornwall\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e384bdd5bc79c6ad9076f62?format=jpeg\" alt=\"jabari jumps\" height=\"2560\" width=\"2205\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"Jabari Jumps\" by Gaia Cornwall, available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0763678384/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0763678384&#38;linkId=7e152d417d48d053b1273be9f1933d5a\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $13.99 and <a href=\"https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/jabari-jumps-gaia-cornwall/1124363212?ean=9780763678388\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $15.49</h3><p>It's not always easy for kids to process their emotions, and fear is a BIG one. Jabari's dad is thoughtful and supportive while Jabari reckons with the high diving board, and we get to see how he eventually meets his goal from different perspectives at the pool. A quick and easy read about perseverance, this would be a great tool for talking to your little one about confronting their own fears.</p>\n\t\"Fry Bread: A Native American Family Story\" by Kevin Noble Maillard\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e384df05bc79c4f4c183d0b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"fry bread a native american family story\" height=\"2557\" width=\"2560\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"Fry Bread: A Native American Family Story\" by Kevin Noble Maillard available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1626727465/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=1626727465&#38;linkId=f9015434ef5a895d1592af1d6419373f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $12.99 and <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/fry-bread-kevin-noble-maillard/1131296428?\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $16.99</h3><p>A Best Picture Book on about a dozen lists in 2019 and 2020, Maillard and illustrator Juana Martinez-Neal (yes, from No. 4 on this list!) combine simple prose with round, doughy, subtle depictions of all the new and old elements that make fry bread special: color, time, history, art, place, and you, among other things. A deep look at the cultural roots of fry bread, this story is abstract in many ways and the illustrations emanate so much love that even younger toddlers can see that sharing really is caring.</p>\n\t\"The Snowy Day\" by Ezra Jack Keats\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e384fc95bc79c703a28d4d8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"the snowy day amazon\" height=\"2314\" width=\"2560\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"The Snowy Day\" by Ezra Jack Keats available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0670654000/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0670654000&#38;linkId=d645151edb5ab4565047a45ecf885551\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $13.48 and <a href=\"https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/snowy-day-ezra-jack-keats/1100257198?ean=9780670654000\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $16.49</h3><p>Quiet Peter has quite a day enjoying the new snow that has blanketed his neighborhood, but I don't have to tell you that since this book has been a classic since it was first published in 1962. Enjoy this sweet tale of a boy on a snowy city adventure with your kids, or without.</p>\n\t\"A Big Mooncake for Little Star\" by Grace Lin\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e3852385bc79c739b49b155?format=jpeg\" alt=\"a big mooncake for little star\" height=\"1313\" width=\"1688\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"A Big Mooncake for Little Star\" by Grace Lin available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0316404489/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0316404489&#38;linkId=0c5f5fc89bb9895bbb2cbec89d3f3fb7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $15.11 and <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/a-big-mooncake-for-little-star-grace-lin/1127581253?\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $16.99</h3><p>Written as a way to share the importance of the Asian holiday Mid Autumn Moon Festival with Lin's own daughter, the focus of this story is Little Star's love affair with the big mooncake her mama made. When Mama eventually discovers that the once full moon(cake) has been whittled down to a crescent before being completely consumed, you can almost feel her quiet joy. The black pages of this book create an all-consuming backdrop for the bright yellow of Little Star's pajamas, blanket, and later, her crumbs.</p>\n\t\"Sofia Valdez, Future Prez\" by Andrea Beaty\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e38533f5bc79c656c3ffaa7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"sofia valdez future prez\" height=\"1216\" width=\"1000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"Sofia Valdez, Future Prez\" by Andrea Beaty available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/141973704X/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=141973704X&#38;linkId=2d4fa3c9f44b392166afd2a3c2a0281d\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $15.03 and <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/sofia-valdez-future-prez-andrea-beaty/1130632033?\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $16.99</h3><p>Sofia serves as a wonderful example for young friends wondering how they can make a difference in their communities, and how to motivate others to believe in you as much as you believe in yourself. I love the intersectionality of this story and others in this series from Beaty and illustrator David Roberts, including <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Ada-Twist-Scientist-Andrea-Beaty/dp/1419721372//ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=158089772X&#38;linkId=1715373b9f2032a5246eceae7c956c53\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Ada Twist, Scientist</a>, which features a young black girl who loves solving mysteries in science.</p>\n\t\"We Are Grateful: Otsaliheliga\" by Traci Sorell\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e3854d05bc79c589d1be697?format=jpeg\" alt=\"we are grateful otsaliheliga\" height=\"2560\" width=\"2363\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"We Are Grateful: Otsaliheliga\" by Traci Sorell available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/158089772X/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=158089772X&#38;linkId=1715373b9f2032a5246eceae7c956c53\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $14.49</h3><p>This is a <em>very</em> loaded book that features Cherokee vocabulary words, including their phonetic pronunciations, symbols, and English translations. Told chronologically, this story and the accompanying illustrations depict how a Cherokee family adapts with the changing seasons, including what they celebrate, eat, plant, and create. Younger children will love looking at all the busy people, while older children may have an easier time relating to the book's discussion of gratitude.</p>\n\t\"The King of Kindergarten\" by Derrick Barnes\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e3855ac5bc79c788951ce79?format=jpeg\" alt=\"the king of kindergarten\" height=\"2560\" width=\"2310\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"The King of Kindergarten\" by Derrick Barnes, available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1524740748/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=1524740748&#38;linkId=8b7471a3b8b185ed6ebe42e638cb9bff\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $11.99</h3><p>This bright, fun story piles on themes of self-esteem about as high as they can go. Barnes' prose helps young friends feel confident and ready for kindergarten, with palpable excitement about the day. He offers a brief glimpse at the structure of a real-life school day, which I also love for my almost-kindergartener. Modeled by the eponymous King, this is a strong lesson in self-confidence, via an author who has made a career of empowering young black children through his literature.</p>\n\t\"The Proudest Blue\" by Ibtihaj Muhammad with S.K. Ali\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e3856605bc79c7986039df3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"the proudest blue\" height=\"595\" width=\"595\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Barnes &#38; Noble</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"The Proudest Blue\" by Ibtihaj Muhammad with S.K. Ali, available at <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Proudest-Blue/dp/1783449721/ref=tmm_pap_swatch_0?_encoding=UTF8&#38;qid=&#38;sr=ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0316519006&#38;linkId=557cf2f458f071afef3921a0edd20702\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon</a> for $16.57 or <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/the-proudest-blue-ibtihaj-muhammad/1130502235?\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $15.99</h3><p>Muhammad is known largely for being the first woman to wear a hijab while competing for the United States in the Olympics, and now she can add storyteller to her list of achievements. Unsurprisingly, this story is all about pride, in yourself and your heritage, as our main character, Faizah, watches her sister wear her first hijab on the first day of a new school year. I love the delicate descriptions of the experience of wearing your first hijab, and the bright, almost emotional illustrations that are paired with them.</p>\n\t\"Last Stop on Market Street\" by Matt de la Peña\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e38577c5bc79c5baa592057?format=jpeg\" alt=\"last stop on market street\" height=\"2560\" width=\"2084\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>\"Last Stop on Market Street\" by Matt de la Pe&#241;a, available at&#160;<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0399257748/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipf_020320_diverse-books-for-young-children-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=0399257748&#38;linkId=8793d81fbd4ea3b6a7ed702580739e80\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-amzn-asin=\"0399257748\" data-ml-dynamic=\"true\" data-ml-dynamic-type=\"sl\">Amazon</a> for $14.42 and <a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/last-stop-on-market-street-matt-de-la-pe-a/1119711662?\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-ml-dynamic=\"true\" data-ml-dynamic-type=\"sl\" data-orig-url=\"https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/last-stop-on-market-street-matt-de-la-pe-a/1119711662\" data-ml-id=\"12\" data-ml=\"true\" data-xid=\"fr1591024273068gha\" data-skimlinks-tracking=\"xid:fr1591024273068gha\">Barnes &#38; Noble</a> for $16.99</h3><p>Precocious CJ has a lot of big, important questions for his grandmother during the trip back to their neighborhood after church. His experience is different (and in many cases, more difficult) than others', but his grandmother replies with optimism and her deep laugh. CJ has many opportunities to interact with a wide variety of people &#8212; the blind person who hears and smells their way around the city, for example &#8212; and it is not lost on me the value of having conversations about privilege and perspective with my own city babies. This author/illustrator team released another subtly challenging story in 2018, \"<a href=\"https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/carmela-full-of-wishes-matt-de-la-pe-a/1127834111?ean=9780399549045\" 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"First-term Republican Dan Crenshaw faces off against Sima Ladjevardian in Texas' 2nd District","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/texas-2nd-district-house-election-dan-crenshaw-sima-ladjevardian-2020","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f53e80be6ff30001d4e750b?format=jpeg\" alt=\" Sima Ladjevardian\" height=\"1000\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Sima Ladjevardian is the Democratic nominee challenging Dan Crenshaw in 2020\n<p class=\"copyright\">Michelle Watson/WireImage via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Representative <strong>Dan Crenshaw&#160;</strong>is facing off against<strong> Democrat Sima Ladjevardian </strong>in Texas' 2nd Congressional District.</li>\n<li>Crenshaw, a former Navy SEAL and a prominent rising star in Republican politics, is seeking a second term running against <strong>Ladjevardian, an attorney and Democratic political strategist.&#160;</strong></li>\n<li>Texas' 2nd District, located in the Houston area, heavily favors Republicans but has shown signs of trending towards Democrats in the past several cycles.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>First-term Republican Representative <strong>Dan Crenshaw&#160;</strong>is facing off against<strong> Sima Ladjevardian&#160;</strong>in Texas' 2nd Congressional District, located in the Houston area.&#160;</p><h2>The candidates</h2><p>Crenshaw, a former Navy SEAL and congressional staffer, won the 2018 election to replace former <strong>Rep. Ted Poe.&#160;</strong></p><p>Crenshaw is a native Houstonian who served in Afghanistan as a Lieutenant Commander on SEAL Team 3 and was wounded in action in Afghanistan, losing all vision in his right eye and having his sight in his left eye severely damaged. After a tough recovery, Crenshaw completed two more deployments with the SEALs before retiring in 2016, receiving a Purple Heart and numerous other awards.&#160;</p><p>In Congress, Crenshaw serves on the powerful House Budget and House Homeland Security Committees. He's also a staunch conservative and ally of President Donald Trump, <a href=\"https://crenshawforcongress.com/policies_issues/\">with his campaign platform</a> emphasizing protecting gun rights, border security, and promoting free-market economic and healthcare policies.&#160;</p><p>Crenshaw is widely considered a rising star in the Republican party. An adept user of social media, he boasts approximately 3.5 million followers between his Facebook, Instagram, and Twitter accounts, is the author of \"Fortitude: American Resilience in the Era of Outrage,\" and recently spoke at the 2020 Republican National Convention.&#160;</p><p>Ladjevardian immigrated to the United States from Iran as a child, is an attorney, breast cancer survivor, and Democratic political strategist. She worked as a Senior Advisor and the Finance Chair for former Rep. Beto O'Rourke's 2018 US Senate campaign against Republican Sen. Ted Cruz.&#160;</p><p>Her <a href=\"https://www.simafortx.com/issues\">campaign platform</a> highlights expanding access to affordable healthcare, including creating a public option to allow Americans to buy into Medicare, combatting climate change and protecting the Houston area from flooding, and improving the US immigration system.&#160;</p><h2>The district</h2><p><a href=\"https://www.govtrack.us/congress/members/TX/2\">Located entirely within Harris County</a>, the 2nd district snakes around the city of Houston from the suburbs northeast of the city, including Kingwood, Humble, and Spring, and then hooks down to encompass some of the areas in western and downtown Houston, including the neighborhood where Rice University is located.&#160;</p><p>The district has shown signs of trending towards Democrats in the past several cycles.</p><p>The district, under its current lines, voted for 2012 Republican presidential nominee Mitt Romney by a margin of 27 percentage points, 63% to 36%, but voted for Trump in 2016 by a considerably smaller margin of nine points, 52% to 43%, <a href=\"https://www.dailykos.com/stories/2012/11/19/1163009/-Daily-Kos-Elections-presidential-results-by-congressional-district-for-the-2012-2008-elections\">according to the Daily Kos</a>, making it the only Houston-area district to vote for Trump.&#160;</p><p>And in 2018, Cruz carried the district by a margin of just one percentage point, 50% to 49%, over O'Rourke <a href=\"https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1W_GTNylAZfboZkDeMsJPGlir3aQB64SzlVHjY9Xdnkk/edit#gid=562073942\">in his reelection campaign that&#160;</a>year as Crenshaw won his first election by seven points over his Democratic opponent.&#160;</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">&#8212;Sima Ladjevardian  (@SimaforTX) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1298828227931246592?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">August 27, 2020</a></blockquote><script async src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>&#160;</p><h2>The money race</h2><p>Crenshaw is one of the most prolific and talented fundraisers in the House Republican caucus. <a href=\"https://www.opensecrets.org/races/summary?cycle=2020&id=TX02&spec=Np;spec=N\">According to the Center for Responsive Politics</a>, he's brought in $9.2 million so far this cycle, spent $5.2 million, and has $4 million cash on hand.&#160;</p><p>Ladjevardian has raised $1.6 million, spent $1.1 million, and has $545,000 in cash on hand so far, nearly eight times less than Crenshaw.&#160;</p><h2>What some of the experts say&#160;</h2><p><a href=\"https://cookpolitical.com/ratings/house-race-ratings\">The Cook Political Report</a>, <a href=\"https://insideelections.com/ratings/house\">Inside Elections</a>, and <a href=\"http://centerforpolitics.org/crystalball/2020-house/\">Sabato's Crystal Ball at the University of Virginia Center for Politics</a> all rate this race as \"likely Republican.\"&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"expanded-coverage\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-source=\"insider-voter-guide\" 03:11:31","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:31","title":"33 high-paying jobs for people who don't like stress","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/33-high-paying-jobs-for-people-who-dont-like-stress-2019-3","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5c80004926289873dd5de6ec?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Square Roots farmers\" height=\"3648\" width=\"4864\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Agricultural engineers are well-compensated while tending to work in low-stress environments.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Square Roots</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>October 10 is <a href=\"https://www.who.int/campaigns/world-mental-health-day\">World Mental Health Day</a>, and it's important to have a job that supports efforts to stay well.</li>\n<li>There are many jobs that are both well-paid and offer a relaxing work environment.</li>\n<li>Using data from the Department of Labor and Bureau of Labor Statistics, we found 33 jobs with annual salaries over $75,000 that also offer a relatively low-stress work situation.</li>\n<li>Highly ranked low-stress well-paying jobs include material scientists, mathematicians, and geographers.</li>\n<li>If you're struggling, call the SAMHSA National Helpline, 1-800-662-HELP (4357), or reach out to the Crisis Text Line by texting HOME to 741741.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories.</a></li>\n</ul><p>October 10 is <a href=\"https://www.who.int/campaigns/world-mental-health-day\">World Mental Health Day</a>, and it is important for people to work in a job that values and supports mental health.</p><p>\"The workplace can be a key location for activities designed to improve wellbeing among adults,\" the <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/workplacehealthpromotion/tools-resources/pdfs/WHRC-Mental-Health-and-Stress-in-the-Workplac-Issue-Brief-H.pdf\">CDC</a> wrote in a 2018 guide of mental health at work.</p><p>Intense, high-stress jobs where you might face a lot of pressure aren't right for everyone.</p><p>Fortunately, for those who would like to work under more relaxing conditions, there are plenty of high-paying jobs that also tend to offer low-stress work environments.</p><p>The Department of Labor's <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/\">O*NET Online occupational database</a> includes survey-based measurements of how important various skills, activities, and personal traits are for a particular job. One of the characteristics measured is <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/find/descriptor/result/1.C.4.b?a=1\">stress tolerance</a>, which O*NET describes as jobs requiring \"accepting criticism and dealing calmly and effectively with high-stress situations.\"</p><p>O*NET scores job characteristics like stress tolerance on a scale from 0 to 100, where a 0 means stress tolerance is not at all necessary for an occupation, and 100 suggests a job with a very high-stress environment.</p><p>We ranked occupational groups from most to least stressful using O*NET's stress tolerance score, with lower scores indicating less stressful jobs. Since we are interested in high-paying jobs, we looked at occupations with average annual salaries of at least $75,000, according to the <a href=\"https://www.bls.gov/oes/\">Bureau of Labor Statistics' Occupational Employment Statistics</a> data for May 2019, the most recently available release.</p><p>Several of the jobs fell in academia, with postsecondary teachers in various fields and researchers in economics, statistics, mathematics, and materials science dominating the top of the list.</p><p>Here are 33 high-paying low-stress jobs, ranked from most to least stressful, and by average annual wages in the event of a tied stress tolerance score:</p>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\t33. Optometrists\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e2f4bf124306a2e234ffbe2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"optometrist\" height=\"3414\" width=\"4552\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Peathegee Inc/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Importance of stress tolerance:</strong> 70</p><p><strong>Average annual salary:&#160;</strong>$122,980</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/29-1041.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Examine eyes and treat conditions and diseases.&#160;</p>\n\t32. Technical writers\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e2f451a5bc79c2e98747826?format=jpeg\" alt=\"mechanics reading manual\" height=\"3675\" width=\"4900\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reza Estakhrian/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Importance of stress tolerance:</strong> 69</p><p><strong>Average annual salary:&#160;</strong>$76,860</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/27-3042.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Write technical materials, such as equipment manuals, appendices, or operating and maintenance instructions. May assist in layout work.</p>\n\t31. Environmental scientists and specialists\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5af3321baa7eaca5098b46a4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"enviromental scientist\" height=\"1265\" width=\"1687\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Gary Kazanjian/AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Importance of stress tolerance:</strong> 69</p><p><strong>Average annual salary:&#160;</strong>$77,940</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/19-2041.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Conduct research or perform investigations for the purpose of identifying, abating, or eliminating sources of pollutants or hazards that affect either the environment or the health of the population.</p>\n\t30. Financial examiners\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f7f5ec0d5f23d00195951a8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"financial planner\" height=\"1414\" width=\"1886\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">PhotoAlto/Eric Audras/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Importance of stress tolerance:</strong> 69</p><p><strong>Average annual salary:&#160;</strong>$92,330</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/13-2061.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Enforce or ensure compliance with laws and regulations governing financial and securities institutions and financial and real estate transactions.</p>\n\t29. Art directors\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/527c1a8beab8ea946ddf1735?format=jpeg\" alt=\"art director\" height=\"1997\" width=\"2663\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dan Kitwood/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Importance of stress tolerance:</strong> 69</p><p><strong>Average annual salary:&#160;</strong>$109,600</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/27-1011.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Formulate design concepts and presentation approaches for visual communications media, such as print, broadcasting, and advertising.</p>\n\t28. Ship engineers\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e2f4e1562fa8140bb4ef842?format=jpeg\" alt=\"marine engineer\" height=\"4000\" width=\"5333\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Igor-Kardasov/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Importance of stress tolerance:</strong> 68</p><p><strong>Average annual salary:&#160;</strong>$79,540</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/53-5031.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Supervise and coordinate activities of crew engaged in operating and maintaining engines, boilers, deck machinery, and electrical, sanitary, and refrigeration equipment aboard ships.</p>\n\t27. Postsecondary mathematical science teachers\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e2f4eba24306a31b86d06cb?format=jpeg\" alt=\"professor\" height=\"3420\" width=\"4560\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ariel Skelley/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Importance of stress tolerance:</strong> 68</p><p><strong>Average annual salary:&#160;</strong>$86,330</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/25-1022.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Teach courses in math, statistics, and actuarial science.</p>\n\t26.
